[wilderness](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wilderness-exploration)
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat)
[scale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#scale) (1" to 10yd) range
categories are primarily for shooting at bodies of troops or similarly
sized targets.

## Magic

A [magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) or
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can memorize a
number of
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) each
day according to his experience level. He must be fresh and rested and
have access to the appropriate [spell
books](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-books) to memorize any
spell therein. Bereft of his [spell
books](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-books) he cannot
memorize any
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells)!

### Spell Casting from Memory

A memorized spell can be cast at any time but once it has been cast it
is erased from memory. Once erased a spell cannot be cast again until it
is memorized the following day. Notwithstanding this limitation, nothing
prevents a
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) or
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) from memorizing
the same spell several times.

In order to invoke a spell the caster must be free to concentrate,
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) his arms
and hands, speak aloud, and see the target. To do so during
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat) the player must
declare his [intent](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intent) at the
beginning of the [turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).
Casting a spell requires the full
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) so no other action may
be attempted. Furthermore, if the caster is struck by any
[missile](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#missile-fire), blow, or
spell before his own invocation is completed it will be foiled and
erased from memory without being triggered. The referee will adjudicate
whether other interruptions are sufficient to foil a spell.

### Spell Casting from Scrolls

A [magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) or
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can
[cast](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory) a
spell of any spell level directly from a
[scroll](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spellbooks-and-scrolls).
Unless the
[scroll](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spellbooks-and-scrolls) was
penned by his own hand a
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) must
employ a [read magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#read-magic)
spell before he can read a [spell
scroll](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-scrolls). Thereafter,
either [class](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#classes) can read a
[spell scroll](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-scrolls)
without memorizing the spell in advance.
[Casting](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory)
a spell from a
[scroll](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spellbooks-and-scrolls)
invokes the magic at the minimum caster level necessary to memorize the
spell and simultaneously erases the spell from the
[scroll](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spellbooks-and-scrolls).

### Reversible Spells

If a [cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) spell is
noted as reversible, only a chaotic
[anti-cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-anti-cleric) can
use the reverse form and only a lawful
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can use the
proper form. If a
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) spell
is noted as reversible, the reverse form is a separate spell which can
be memorized,
[cast](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory),
and written to a
[scroll](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spellbooks-and-scrolls)
exactly as per any other spell.

### Spell Books

Magic-users and
[clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) begin play
with a book of 1st level
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) but
must find, buy, or
[research](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#researching-new-spells)
higher level spell books thereafter.

Adventuring is a dangerous business so a spell caster may wish to
construct a duplicate spell book to carry without risk to his primary
resource. Should a spell book be
[lost](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#becoming-lost), damaged, or
destroyed in any event it can be replaced at a cost. A book of 1st level
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells)
costs 2,000 gp, a book of 2nd level
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells)
costs 4,000 gp, a book of 3rd level
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells)
costs 8,000 gp, and so on.

### Creating Spell Scrolls

Magic-users and
[clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can copy
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells)
which they can memorize onto
[scrolls](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spellbooks-and-scrolls).
It takes one week to create any [spell
scroll](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-scrolls) and costs 100
gp per spell level. Thus, a 4th level [spell
scroll](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-scrolls) takes one
week to construct at a cost of 400 gp. A [spell
scroll](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-scrolls) can be
invoked only once and is at risk of being ruined by rain, fire, and
other
[dungeon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#populating-a-dungeon)
hazards.

### Researching New Spells

Clerics and
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can
research new
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) for
their repertoires. The spell level of a new spell cannot exceed that
which the researcher is able to memorize. Otherwise, the player can
contrive whatever spell he desires, remembering that the referee will
determine what is allowable and the spell level of the new magic.

Success is a matter of time and investment. One week and 2,000 gp are
required for a 1st level spell. Costs double and time is extended by one
week at each successively higher spell level. Thus, a 2nd level spell
requires two weeks and 4,000 gp, a 3rd level spell requires three weeks
and 8,000 gp, a 4th level spell requires four weeks and 16,000 gp and so
on.

### Cumulative Magic

Spells and other magical effects will usually combine safely with one
another. However, multiple enchantments with the same effect are not
cumulative; only the single, most powerful effect applies.

Delving Deeper Online table1\_20

## Explanation of Spells

#### 1st Level Cleric Spells

##### Cure Light Wounds

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 1 creature, range: touch) The
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can restore 2-7
[lost hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) to
any one creature (including himself) after one
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) of aid. [Hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice)
cannot be raised beyond the creature’s normal total. The reverse, cause
light wounds, will cause 2-7 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) at a touch,
possibly requiring an attack roll to touch an unwilling target.

##### Detect Evil

(affects: self, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 12") The
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can sense the
presence of any enchanted, conjured, supernatural, or undead creature
within range, as well as any
[curse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses) or malicious
enchantment upon an object or place.

##### Detect Magic

(affects: self, duration: 2
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 6") The
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can sense the
presence of any enchantment on a person, place, or object within range
and sight.

##### Light

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 3" diameter, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) + 1
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)/level, range: 12")
Causes an object or volume of
[space](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#space-required) to be lit as
if by torchlight, illuminating a 3" diameter. The reverse, darkness,
creates a 3" diameter sphere of darkness that is impenetrable even to
creatures that see in the dark and to the
[darkvision](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#darkvision) spell, but
not to the [true
seeing](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#true-seeing) spell.

##### Protection from Evil

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: self, duration: 12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)) This spell prevents
any enchanted or conjured creature from contacting the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric). Furthermore,
attacks made against the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) by other
chaotic types will be at −2 to hit and the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) will make
[saving throws](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) at
+2. The reverse, protection from good, applies equally to enchanted or
conjured creatures but protects against lawful rather than chaotic
types.

##### Purify Food and Drink

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
duration: permanent, range: 1") Makes spoiled,
[poisoned](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#poison_1), or
contaminated food, drink, or
[Unholy](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#unholy) water whole and
suitable for consumption. Enough food for one dozen
[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men) or two weeks worth of
rations are affected. The reverse, putrefy food and drink, will instead
spoil food, drink, and [Holy](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#holy)
water.

#### 2nd Level Cleric Spells

##### Bless

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 6" diameter, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 6") The
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) bestows a +1
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
bonus and a +1 benefit to attack rolls upon all allies within 3" who are
not already in [combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat). The
reverse, bane, imposes equivalent penalties upon foes.

##### Continuous Light

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 24" diameter, duration: permanent, range: 12") Causes an object
or volume of [space](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#space-required)
to be lit as if by sunlight.
[Monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2) affected by
sunlight are dazzled but otherwise unharmed. [Continuous
light](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#continuous-light) is
permanent unless dispelled. The reverse, continuous darkness, creates a
permanent, 24" diameter sphere of darkness that is impenetrable even to
creatures that see in the dark and to the
[darkvision](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#darkvision) spell, but
not to the [true
seeing](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#true-seeing) spell.

##### Find Traps

(affects: self, duration: 2
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 3") The
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can sense any
magical or mechanical
[trap](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#tricks-and-traps) within
sight and range. No insight as to how the
[trap](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#tricks-and-traps) might be
deactivated is conveyed.

##### Hold Person

(affects: 1 or 1-4 persons, duration: 9
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 18") 1-4
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) are held
immobile if they fail a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
paralysis](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#paralysis-and-petrification).
If a single [man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) is
targeted his [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) is penalized
by −2.

##### Remove Disease

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 1 creature, duration: permanent, range: touch) Cures the
subject of all natural diseases or one supernatural disease such as
[mummy](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#mummies) rot or lycanthropy.
The reverse, cause disease, infects the subject with any disease known
to the
[anti-cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-anti-cleric) at a
touch, possibly requiring an attack roll to touch an unwilling subject.

##### Speak with Animals

(affects: self, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 3") The
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can communicate
with ordinary animals, including
[giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants)-sized sorts,
receiving answers to questions subject to a
[reaction](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
check. The animals will not attack the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) for the
duration, regardless of their
[reaction](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks),
but will perform a favor or service only if the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) secures a
positive (or better)
[reaction](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks).

#### 3rd Level Cleric Spells

##### Circle of Protection from Evil

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 1" radius, duration: 12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)) As per the
[protection from
evil](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#protection-from-evil) spell,
except that the protection extends to a 1" radius around the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric).

##### Cure Serious Wounds

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 1 creature, range: touch) The
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can restore
4-14 [lost hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) to
any one creature (including himself) after one
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) of aid. [Hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice)
cannot be raised beyond the creature’s normal total. The reverse, cause
serious wounds, will cause 4-14 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) at a touch,
possibly requiring an attack roll to touch an unwilling target.

##### Enervate Dead

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 4-48 undead, duration: 7-12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 12")
Temporarily paralyzes
[skeletons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#skeletons) and
[zombies](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#zombies) with no [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) allowed. 2-12
undead are enervated for every three whole levels the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) has. Thus a 6th
level [cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can
enervate 4-24 undead, a 9th level
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can enervate
6-36 undead, and a 12th level
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can enervate
8-48 undead. The reverse, [animate
dead](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#animate-dead), causes nearby
bones or bodies to rise as half as many undead
[skeletons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#skeletons) or
[zombies](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#zombies) under the
[anti-cleric’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-anti-cleric)
command. They will obey until destroyed in
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat), by a [dispel
magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-magic), or by a
[dispel evil](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-evil) spell.

##### Locate Object

(affects: self, duration: 2
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 9" +
1"/level) The [cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric)
can sense the direction to a well known or clearly visualized object
within range. If more than one object of the visualized sort is in range
only the nearest is located. A specific unique object can only be sought
by this spell if the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) has previously
observed the object firsthand.

##### Remove Curse

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 1 [curse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses),
duration: permanent, range: touch) Lifts one
[curse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses) from a creature or
object, causing the latter to become a normal, unenchanted item of its
type. The reverse, bestow
[curse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses), burdens the subject
with any [curse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses) so named by
the [anti-cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-anti-cleric).
Note that a lawful
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) must specify
only lawful [curses](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses).

##### Speak with Dead

(affects: self, duration: special, range: 3") An echo of life is
bestowed upon the remains of a deceased creature within range so that it
can answer 1-6 questions asked by the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric), subject to a
usual
[reaction](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
check. This spell has no effect if the remains have been deceased longer
than one week per level of the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric).

#### 4th Level Cleric Spells

##### Control Water

(affects: 1 body of water, duration: 12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 24") The
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) causes the
water level of a river or similar body of water to immediately fall to
half its natural depth within 24" of himself, allowing a waterway to be
forded, or to rise to half its depth again, precipitating a flash
flooding.

##### Create Food and Drink

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: special, range: 1") Creates wholesome food and drink sufficient
to feed three [men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men) (or one
[horse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#horses) or
[mule](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#horses)) for each of the
[cleric’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) experience
levels. The reverse, destroy food and drink, turns a like amount of food
and drink to ash.

##### Cure Critical Wounds

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 1 creature, range: touch) The
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can restore
6-21 [lost hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) to
any one creature (including himself) after one
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) of aid. [Hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice)
cannot be raised beyond the creature’s normal total. The reverse, cause
critical wounds, will cause 6-21 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) at a touch,
possibly requiring an attack roll to touch an unwilling target.

##### Hold Monster

(affects: 1 or 1-4 creatures, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) + 1
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)/level, range: 12") 1-4
creatures are held immobile if they fail a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
paralysis](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#paralysis-and-petrification).
If a single creature is targeted its [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) is penalized
by −2.

##### Neutralize Poison

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 1 poison, duration: permanent, range: 1") A glass of
[poisoned](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#poison_1) wine, a
venomous [monster](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2), an
envenomed weapon, or any other poison is rendered non-toxic but this
spell will not reverse the effect of a
[poisoning](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#poison_1) that has
already occurred. The reverse, poison, will cause any food or drink to
become deadly poison or any object or creature to become venomous.

##### Speak with Plants

(affects: self, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 3") The
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can communicate
with ordinary plants and supernatural plant types. He can receive
answers to questions subject to a
[reaction](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
check. The plants will not attack the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) for the
duration, regardless of their
[reaction](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks),
but will perform a favor or service only if the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) secures a
positive (or better)
[reaction](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks).

#### 5th Level Cleric Spells

##### Commune

(affects: self, duration: special) The
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) seeks divinely
given knowledge. The Gods, or their agents, will entertain 1-6 questions
with a simple “yes” or “no” answer which will be absolute. Use of this
spell is limited to once per adventure, or even more infrequently, for
the Gods dislike frequent interruptions. However, on the most
[Holy](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#holy) day of the year three
six-sided [dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-dice_1) are
thrown with the highest result being the number of questions that will
be answered.

##### Dispel Evil

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 1 enchantment, duration: permanent, range: 3") Immediately
dismisses all enchanted or conjured creatures and
[curses](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses) or enchantments of
a malign sort within 3". Animated dead are destroyed while conjured
[insect plagues](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#insect-plague),
[djinn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#a-djinni),
[efreet](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#an-efreeti),
[elementals](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals), and
[invisible
stalkers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#an-invisible-stalker) are
sent back to their origin. All
[curses](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses) and malign
enchantments within 3" are affected as if by a [dispel
magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-magic). The reverse,
dispel good, functions against enchanted or conjured creatures and
enchantments of the benign sort.

##### Insect Plague

(affects: 40" diameter, duration: 1 day, range: 48") Conjures a vast, 4"
deep swarm of crawling, creeping, and flying insects which
[moves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) at 6"
in a direction indicated by the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) or remains
stationary. The swarm obscures vision, impedes
[movement](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2), and
devours all organic material including crops. Smoke, fire, or extreme
cold will temporarily delay or divert the swarm but not destroy it.
[Normal-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types) will
automatically flee but those caught in the plague will suffer
innumerable bites and stings amounting to 1 point of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) per
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat)
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), regardless of
[armor](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields). Misuse
of this spell will cause a
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) to immediately
become an
[anti-cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-anti-cleric).

##### Quest

(affects: 1 subject, duration: special, range: 3") The subject is
compelled to perform a quest specified by the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric). Upon bestowing
a quest the [cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric)
also specifies a [curse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses).
Should the subject dally or deviate from his quest he will be afflicted
by the [curse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses) until he
resumes the quest. Only the completion of the quest or a successful
[dispel evil](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-evil) (or
dispel good) will end this spell. Note that a lawful
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) must specify
only lawful quests and
[curses](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses).

##### Raise Dead

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 1 person, duration: permanent, range: touch) Restores life to a
deceased [man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) who
has not been dead any longer than one day per level of the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric). Rising from
the dead is a great ordeal and the subject must make a successful [shock
survival](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#shock-survival) check in
order to be raised. Should this check succeed he returns to life but
requires two weeks of recuperation. The reverse, finger of death, causes
a baleful ray to issue from the
[anti-cleric’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-anti-cleric)
pointed finger to any
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) within sight
and 12" range. If the target makes a successful [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
wands](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wands-and-rays) the effect is
negated; otherwise, he dies instantly.

##### True Seeing

(affects: self, duration: 11-16
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)) The
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) sees all things
as they actually are. Blindness and darkness (even the magical sort) are
defeated. [Traps](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#tricks-and-traps),
[secret doors](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#secret-doors),
invisible creatures, and hidden object are plainly seen.
[Illusions](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#illusions) and charms
are immediately discerned as is the true nature of any
[polymorphed](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#baleful-polymorph),
petrified, or transmuted creature or object.

#### 1st Level Magic-User Spells

##### Alter Self

(affects: self, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) + 1
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)/level) The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can
assume the appearance of any creature of the same general size and shape
as himself. He could appear to be a town guard, a beautiful maiden, or a
[gnoll](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#gnolls) but not a
[horse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#horses) or a
[wyvern](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wyverns).

##### Charm Person

(affects: 1 person, duration: special, range: 12") Brings a single
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) who fails to
save [versus spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell)
completely under the influence of the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user). Gross
abuse or negligence allows the
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) another
[saving throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws);
otherwise, the charm lasts until it is lifted by the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) or
dispelled.

##### Color Spray

(affects: 12" arc, duration: 2-12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)) 2-7 seeing creatures
are rendered unconscious by a dazzling glare of clashing colors. Those
nearest to the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) are
always affected first, sheltering those farther back.
[Heroic-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types) are
allowed a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell) to negate the effect
and
[superheroic-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
are unaffected.

##### Comprehend Languages

(affects: self, duration: special) Enables the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) to read
any [language](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#many-languages),
cipher, message, map, or other written instruction excepting magical
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) or
command words. The spell lasts long enough to read two short writings or
one longer one, but no power to speak or
[listen](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#listening) is conferred.

##### Detect Magic

(affects: self, duration: 2
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 6") The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can
sense the presence of any enchantment on a person, place, or object
within range and sight.

##### Fog Wall

(affects: 6" wall, duration: special, range: 12"): Conjures a bank of
thick fog which persists for as long as the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
concentrates on maintaining it. The fog wall is 20ft thick and up to 6"
long and 20ft high (or any equivalent dimensions) and is straight or
curved as the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
desires. It is impenetrable to sight.

##### Gazeback

(affects: self, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)) The
[magic-user’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) eyes
become mirrored granting him immunity to dazzling and gaze attacks
without impairing his sight. The gaze attacks of
[basilisks](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#basilisks),
[medusae](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#medusae), and
[vampires](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#vampires), the [mirror of
life
trapping](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#mirror-of-life-trapping),
and the [color spray](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#color-spray)
spell are all defeated. Moreover, any gaze attack attempted within 3"
will be reflected back at the attacker exactly as if they had looked
into a mirror.

##### Hold Portal

(affects: 1 portal, duration: 2-12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 1") Holds one
[door](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#doors), gate,
[window](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#window), shutter, or other
portal securely fast exactly as though it were locked. The portal can
then be opened only by a magic-using creature with at least 7 [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice), a
[knock](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#knock) spell, a [dispel
magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-magic), or a
resourceful
[thief](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-thief-optional-class)
(if these are used).

##### Light

(affects: 3" diameter, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) + 1
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)/level, range: 12")
Causes an object or volume of
[space](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#space-required) to be lit as
if by torchlight, illuminating a 3" diameter.

##### Protection from Evil

(affects: self, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)) This spell prevents
any enchanted or conjured creature from contacting the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user).
Furthermore, attacks made against the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) by
other chaotic types will be at −2 to hit and the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) will
make [saving throws](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws)
at +2.

##### Read Magic

(affects: self, duration: special) Enables the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) to
decipher
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) on
[scrolls](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spellbooks-and-scrolls) or
in [spell books](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-books), or
magical inscriptions or command words on other objects. The spell lasts
long enough to comprehend two short writings or one longer one.
[Spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells)
written by other
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) are
incomprehensible without the use of this spell.

##### Sleep

(affects: 1 or 4-14 creatures, duration: 3-18
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 24") Causes
4-14 [normal-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types) or
1 [heroic-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types) with
up to 4+1 [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) to
fall into a fitful slumber. The magic is indiscriminate and must affect
the indicated number of creatures beginning with those nearest the
target. The magic affects only creatures that normally sleep but no
[saving throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) is
allowed.

#### 2nd Level Magic-User Spells

##### Continuous Light

(affects: 24" diameter, duration: permanent, range: 12") Causes an
object or volume of
[space](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#space-required) to be lit as
if by torchlight, illuminating a 24" diameter. [Continuous
light](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#continuous-light) is
permanent unless dispelled.

##### Darkvision

(affects: 1 creature, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) + 1
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)/level, range: touch)
The subject can see up to 6" in darkness.

##### Detect Invisibility

(affects: self, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 1"/level) The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can
plainly see invisible, hidden, ghostly, or otherwise transparent
creatures and objects within range and line of sight.

##### Invisibility

(affects: 1 target, duration: special, range: 24") One object or
creature becomes invisible. If the subject takes overtly hostile action
the spell is ended immediately; otherwise, it lasts indefinitely. Note
that [fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) of 8th
level and above will sense invisible opponents within 3" even without
seeing them.

##### Knock

(affects: portals, range: 6") Opens all known and unlocked
[doors](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#doors),
[windows](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#window), gates, and other
portals within range, or exactly one such portal which is known to exist
but is stuck, barred, locked, or magically held.

##### Levitate

(affects: self, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) + 1
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)/level) The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
levitates up or down as desired at a rate of 6". The spell will not
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) him
laterally, although he might still clamber along a cliff face or ceiling
with his hands at a rate of 3".

##### Locate Object

(affects: self, duration: 2
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 6" +
1"/level) The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can
sense the direction to a well known or clearly visualized object within
range. If more than one object of the visualized sort is in range only
the nearest is located. A specific unique object can only be sought by
this spell if the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) has
previously observed the object firsthand.

##### Phantasm

(affects: 3" diameter, duration: concentration, range: 24") Creates a
convincing, animated phantasm that persists for as long as the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
continues to concentrate on controlling it. A [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell) is allowed each
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) that someone doubts
the phantasm’s veracity. A successful [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) enables them
to end the phantasm by purposefully touching it. Otherwise, the phantasm
is considered “real” for all purposes including causing real
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage).

##### Protection from Missiles

(affects: 1 creature, duration: 12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 3") The
subject is granted invulnerability to ordinary
[missiles](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#missile-fire) including
[spears](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spears), stones,
[arrows](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#arrows-and-bolts), and
[bolts](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#arrows-and-bolts). This
protection does not extend to artillery shot, boulders hurled by
[giants](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants), ordinary
[missiles](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#missile-fire) fired by
[heroic-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types), or
enchanted [missiles](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#missile-fire)
of any sort.

##### Sixth Sense

(affects: self, duration: 12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 6") The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
concentrates on a specific direction for one
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) in order to sense what
creatures are within range in that direction. Having sensed creatures,
the [magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can
perceive the surface thoughts of any one creature at a time,
[listening](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#listening) in for as
long as desired. He can hop from creature to creature as desired,
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) by
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), unless the magic is
obstructed by lead or any rock thicker than 20ft.

##### Web

(affects: 2" diameter or 3"×1", duration: permanent, range: 3") Fills
the targeted area to 10ft depth with strong, sticky, inflammable fibers.
Creatures at the edge are allowed a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus breath
weapon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) to avoid
entanglement but those that are wholly surrounded cannot avoid it.
[Giants](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants) and similarly
powerful creatures can tear through the web in a single
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), as can a flaming
sword cut through its fibers.
[Ogres](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ogres),
[trolls](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#trolls), and
[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men) with 18
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) can tear
through it in two [turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).
[Normal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types)
[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men) require four
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) of toil to tear
through the web while lesser creatures will be held fast.

##### Witch Lock

(affects: 1 portal, duration: permanent, range: 1") As per a [hold
portal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#hold-portal) spell except
that a witch lock lasts indefinitely and can be placed on anything that
can be opened including chests, draws, wardrobes, flasks, books, and
portals. A [knock](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#knock) spell or
the [magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) who
created the witch lock can bypass it without ending the spell, as can
any other
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) at
least three levels higher than the caster.

#### 3rd Level Magic-User Spells

##### Circle of Invisibility

(affects: 1" radius, duration: special, range: 24") All creatures within
1" of the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user), or any
point within sight and range, are affected as per the
[invisibility](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#invisibility) spell.
The spell does not enable affected creatures to see one another.

##### Circle of Protection from Evil

(affects: 1" radius, duration: 12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)) As per the
[protection from
evil](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#protection-from-evil) spell
except that the protection extends to a 1" radius about the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user).

##### Clairvoyance

(affects: self, duration: 12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 6") The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can see
in his mind’s eye anywhere he desires within range except that the spell
is obstructed by lead or any rock thicker than 20ft.

##### Dispel Magic

(affects: 1 enchantment, duration: permanent, range: 12") Ends any
ongoing spell that was begun by a caster of equal or lower level. If the
ongoing spell was begun by a higher level caster there is a 10% chance
for each level he has over and above the
[magic-user’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) level
that the dispel magic will fail. Instantaneous
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells)
cannot be dispelled, nor will this spell affect magic items.

##### Fireball

(affects: 2" radius, duration: instantaneous, range: 24") The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) points
his finger at a target anywhere within range and sight and causes a
fiery explosion to fill a 2" radius, or an equivalent volume of
available [space](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#space-required)
(twelve 10ft cubes on a typical
[dungeon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#populating-a-dungeon)
map). Everyone caught within the blast suffers 1-6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) per level of the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) to a
maximum of 10-60 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice). A
successful [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus breath
weapon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) will reduce
this [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) by half.

##### Fly

(affects: self, duration: 1-6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) + 1
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)/level) Enables the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) to fly
at a [movement
rate](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#movement-rates_1) up to 12".
The spell duration is determined secretly by the referee.

##### Haste

(affects: 4-24 creatures, duration: 3
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 24") 4-24
creatures within a 4" diameter are quickened. Affected creatures will
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) at
double pace and, against any non-quickened creature, will always gain
[initiative](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#initiative) and have a
+2 to hit adjustment. Those nearest to the target are always affected
first. At the end of the spell each affected creature must save [versus
petrification](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#paralysis-and-petrification)
or else age one year. [Haste](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#haste)
counters [slow](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#slow) and vice
versa.

##### Hold Person

(affects: 1 or 1-4 persons, duration: 1-6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) + 1
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)/level, range: 12") 1-4
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) are held
immobile if they fail a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
paralysis](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#paralysis-and-petrification).
If a single [man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) is
targeted his [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) is penalized
by −2.

##### Lightning Bolt

(affects: 6", duration: instantaneous, range: 18") Unleashes a stroke of
lightning at any target in range and sight. It passes directly through
creatures but reflects off hard surfaces, possibly even doubling back,
so that it is always 6" long; thus the maximum reach of this spell is up
to 24". Everyone passed through suffers 1-6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice)
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) per level of the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) to a
maximum of 10-60 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice). A
successful [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
wands](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wands-and-rays) will reduce
this [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) by half.

##### Plant Growth

(affects: 30"×30" or 33" diameter, duration: permanent, range: 12")
Causes existing vegetation within a 33" diameter (or equivalent area) to
become absurdly overgrown and virtually impassable. The growth lasts
until it is hacked or burned away or until it is dispelled.

##### Slow

(affects: 4-24 creatures, duration: 3
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 24") 4-24
creatures within a 4" diameter are slowed. Affected creatures will
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) at half
pace and, against any non-slowed creature, will always lose
[initiative](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#initiative) and have a
−2 to hit adjustment. Those nearest to the target are always affected
first. Slow counters [haste](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#haste)
and vice versa.

##### Water Breathing

(affects: 1 creature, duration: 12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 3") The
targeted creature is empowered to breathe normally under water. No
buoyancy or ability to
[swim](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#swimming) is conferred.

#### 4th Level Magic-User Spells

##### Animal Growth

(affects: 1-6 animals, duration: 12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 12") Causes
1-6 ordinary animals within range and sight to grow to
[giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants) size, assuming all
of the game statistics of the
[giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants) sort. If no such
statistics are given assume that size and [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) are
doubled. The disposition of the animals toward the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) is
unaffected by this spell.

##### Animate Dead

(affects: 2-24 dead, duration: permanent, range: 3") Causes nearby bones
or bodies to rise as undead
[skeletons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#skeletons) or
[zombies](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#zombies) under the
[magic-user’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
command. 1-6 undead are animated for every three whole levels the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) has.
Thus a 7th or 8th level
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can
animate 2-12 undead, a 9th, 10th or 11th level
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can
animate 3-18 undead, and a 12th level
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can
animate 4-24 undead. They will obey until destroyed in
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat), by a [dispel
magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-magic), or a [dispel
evil](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-evil) spell.

##### Charm Monster

(affects: 1 or 3-18 creatures, duration: special, range: 12") Brings
3-18 [normal-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types) or
a single
[heroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types)/[superheroic-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
that fails to save [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell) completely under the
influence of the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user). Gross
abuse or negligence allows the
[monster](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2) (or
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2)) an
additional [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws); otherwise,
the charm lasts until it is lifted by the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) or is
dispelled.

##### Confusion

(affects: 3-18 creatures, duration: 12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 12") Causes
confusion in 3-18 creatures. The magic is indiscriminate and must affect
the indicated number of creatures beginning with those nearest to the
target.
[Heroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types)/[superheroic-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
are allowed a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell) to negate the effect;
otherwise, each individual’s behavior is determined randomly each
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

Delving Deeper Online table1\_22

|                              |                                                |
|------------------------------|------------------------------------------------|
| Table 1.22 Confused Behavior |                                                |
| 1-6                          | Behavior                                       |
| 1                            | Stand oblivious, staring off into the distance |
| 2                            | Walk quietly away                              |
| 3                            | Sit and eat whatever is nearby                 |
| 4                            | Shout poetry angrily (or equivilent)           |
| 5                            | Run in a random direction at maximum pace      |
| 6                            | Attack the nearest creature                    |

##### Dimension Door

(affects: 1 subject, duration: instantaneous, range: 1") The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) or
other subject steps from his present location to any destination within
36" specified by
[distance](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#encounter-distance_3) and
direction.

##### Fear

(affects: 6" arc, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 6") Sends a
wave of panic out in an arc before the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) to 6"
range. All
[normal-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types) in the
area of effect will immediately flee for six
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).
[Heroic-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types) are
allowed a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell) to negate the effect.

##### Hallucinatory Terrain

(affects: 160" diameter, duration: special, range: 24") Creates an
illusionary terrain that conceals the underlying geography and is
convincing in every way from a
[distance](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#encounter-distance_3).
The hallucination will not stand up to close inspection, however, and
can be seen through automatically by any intelligent being who examines
it carefully from within.

##### Polymorph

(affects: self, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) + 1
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)/level) Transforms the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) into
any creature he desires. He assumes the size,
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength), mobility,
[armor class](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#melee), and physical
attack and [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage)
capabilities of his new form, excluding supernatural
[abilities](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-abilities)
such as [breath
weapons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon), gaze
attacks, and spell
[casting](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory).
He retains his own
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence), [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice),
[saving throws](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws), and
ability to speak and
[cast](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory)
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells).

##### Remove Curse

(affects: 1 [curse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses),
duration: permanent, range: touch) Lifts one
[curse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses) from a creature or
object causing the latter to become a normal, unenchanted item of its
type.

##### Wall of Fire

(affects: 6" wall, duration: concentration, range: 6") Conjures a
blazing curtain of fire which persists for as long as the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
concentrates upon maintaining it. The wall of fire is 5ft thick and up
to 6" long and 20ft high (or any equivalent dimensions). It can be
straight or curved as the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
desires, including a 10ft high 4" diameter circle. Creatures of fire are
unaffected except by its opaqueness. The wall is otherwise impenetrable
to [normal-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types)
while
[heroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types)/[superheroic-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
suffer 1-6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) for bursting
through. Creatures of cold and undead instead suffer 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice). A
wall of fire and a white [dragon’s
breath](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragon-breath-weapon) (or
blast from a [wand of
ice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wand-of-ice)) will negate one
another, resulting in a double-sized [fog
wall](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fog-wall).

##### Wall of Ice

(affects: 6" wall, duration: permanent, range: 12") Conjures a steaming
cold bulkhead of hard pack ice. The wall of ice is 5ft thick and up to
6" long and 20ft high (or any equivalent dimensions). It can be straight
or curved as the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
desires, including a 10ft high 4" diameter circle. A wall of ice is
opaque and is impenetrable to
[normal-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types).
[Heroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types)/[superheroic-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
can attempt to crash through a wall of ice as they might break down
[doors](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#doors). Any such attempt
causes 1-6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) except to creatures
of cold (who are unharmed) and creatures of fire who instead suffer 2-12
[hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice). A
wall of ice and a red [dragon’s
breath](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragon-breath-weapon) (or
[fireball](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fireball)) will negate
one another, resulting in a double-sized [fog
wall](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fog-wall).

##### Witch Eye

(affects: self, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 1") Conjures
an invisible, floating eye that flies at a rate of 12" per
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) to anywhere the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) desires
within 24". The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can see
in his mind’s eye everything that the witch eye sees.

#### 5th Level Magic-User Spells

##### Baleful Polymorph

(affects: 1 creature, duration: permanent, range: 6") Transforms a
subject within range into any creature the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
desires. The subject must immediately make a [shock
survival](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#shock-survival) check with
failure resulting in death. Otherwise, he assumes the size,
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength), mobility,
[armor class](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#melee), and physical
attack and [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage)
capabilities of the new form including supernatural
[abilities](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-abilities)
such as [breath
weapons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) and gaze
attacks, but excluding spell
[casting](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory).
He retains his own
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence), [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice),
[saving throws](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws), and
ability to speak and
[cast](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory)
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells). The
transformation is permanent until dispelled.

##### Cloudkill

(affects: 3" diameter, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 1") Conjures
a 3" diameter bank of dense,
[poisonous](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#poison) fog which rolls
along the ground at a rate of 3" either with the
[wind](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strong-winds) or away from
the [magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user).
The vapors are heavier than air and will sink to the lowest lay of the
land, pouring down sinkholes or openings for example. Any
[normal-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types) that
breathes the fog is immediately slain.
[Heroic-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types) are
allowed a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
poison](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#poison) to avoid death and
[superheroic-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
are unaffected.

##### Contact Other Plane

(affects: self, duration: special) The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) seeks
knowledge from powerful beings on other planes of existence. These will
answer the
[magic-user’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
questions with a “yes” or “no” answer which will be absolute. 1-6
questions (determined secretly by the referee) will be entertained
safely. For each additional question asked the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) must
make a successful [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell) or be
[feebleminded](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#feeblemind) for 1-6
weeks.

##### Feeblemind

(affects: 1 creature, duration: permanent, range: 24") One intelligent
creature within range and sight must save [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell) at −4 or become a
mental invalid. A feebleminded creature can neither read, write, figure,
communicate in any coherent fashion, nor
[cast](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory)
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) or
use command words. The spell lasts until it is canceled by a [dispel
magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-magic).

##### Hold Monster

(affects: 1 or 1-4 creatures, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) + 1
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)/level, range: 12") 1-4
creatures are held immobile if they fail a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
paralysis](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#paralysis-and-petrification).
If a single creature is targeted its [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) is penalized
by −2.

##### Invoke Elemental

(affects: 1 [elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals),
duration: special, range: 24") Conjures one earth, air, fire, or [water
elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals-water) of the
16 [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) sort.
The [elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals) does the
[magic-user’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) will
until it is destroyed in
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat) or is dismissed by
the [magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) or
a [dispel evil](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-evil). The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) may
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) at half
rate but controlling the
[elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals) requires the
remainder of his concentration. If he should lose concentration (by
being hit, for example) he can no longer dismiss the
[elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals) and it will
attack him immediately. No more than one
[elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals) of each type
can be conjured per day.

##### Magic Jar

(affects: self, duration: special, range: 3") The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) sends
his spirit into a gem, crystal, or similar
[vessel](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#oared-vessels) within 3",
leaving his own body helpless. From there the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can
attempt to possess any creature that approaches within 12". He can
automatically repossess his own body but others are allowed a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell). Should they fail
this [saving throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws)
the [magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
possesses them and assumes full control of their physical faculties
while retaining his own intellect. The
[magic-user’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
spirit can return to the magic jar at any time and automatically does so
if ever the possessed body is slain. If his own body has died in the
meanwhile he is trapped in the magic jar until another body can be
possessed. If the magic jar is destroyed while the
[magic-user’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
spirit is resident, he is utterly annihilated and cannot be raised or
reincarnated.

##### Passwall

(affects: 1" tunnel, duration: 3
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 3") Opens a
tunnel up to 5ft in diameter and 1" deep through any wall—including
solid rock but excluding solid iron.

##### Telekinesis

(affects: 20lb/level, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 12") Any
object or objects (including living things) within sight and range whose
total mass does not exceed 20lb per level of the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can be
moved by thought alone. Objects can be moved from anywhere within range
to anywhere else within range in a single
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### Teleport

(affects: 1 subject, duration: instantaneous, range: touch) Instantly
transports the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) (or
other subject) from place to place regardless of
[distance](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#encounter-distance_3),
possibly requiring an attack roll to touch an unwilling subject. The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) must be
very familiar with the destination or risk an error. If he is only
passingly familiar with the destination an error will occur with a throw
of 1 on a six-sided die. If he has only seen the destination once an
error will occur with a throw of 1-2. If he has never seen the
destination an error will occur with a throw of 1-3. When an error
occurs the subject will arrive either 10-60ft too high or too low (50%
chance of either). Teleporting into mid-air results in a
[fall](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#falling); teleporting into
solid earth results in death.

##### Transmute Rock to Mud

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 30"×30" or 33" diameter, duration: 3-18 days, range: 12")
Transmutes a large area of rock or earth into a 10ft deep mud slough,
undermining structures,
[drowning](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#drowning) heavy
creatures, and otherwise reducing
[movement](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) to
3". The mud will dry after 3-18 days leaving the rock or earth in its
former state. Transmute rock to mud can be canceled immediately by a
transmute mud to rock spell and vice versa.

##### Wall of Stone

(affects: 6" wall, duration: permanent, range: 6") Conjures an imposing
bulkhead of solid stone 5ft thick and up to 6" long and 20ft high (or
any equivalent dimensions). It can be plain or featured and straight or
curved, as the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
desires, including a 10ft high 4" diameter circle. It is impenetrable to
all but the ordinary means of tunneling or battery, except that it can
be dismissed by a [dispel
magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-magic).

#### 6th Level Magic-User Spells

##### Anti-Magic Shield

(affects: self, duration: 12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)) An invisible barrier
surrounds the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) so that
no spell or spell-like effect (including charms and gaze attacks) may
pass in either direction for the duration. It is impervious even to
[dispel magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-magic).

##### Control Water

(affects: 1 body of water, duration: 12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 24") The
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) causes
the water level of a river or similar body of water within 24" of
himself to immediately fall to half its natural depth (allowing a
waterway to be forded) or to rise to half its depth again (precipitating
a flash flooding).

##### Control Weather

(affects: 1 geographic region, duration: permanent) Invokes a single
desired [weather](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#weather) condition
in the local geographical region the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) is in.
The [weather](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#weather) condition may
be extreme but must be naturally occurring. The
[weather](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#weather) will take 1-6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) to change but will
then last until dispelled.

##### Disintegrate

(affects: 1 target, range: 6") A deadly beam of darkness irrevocably
disintegrates any single non-magical object or creature. Creatures are
allowed a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
wands](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wands-and-rays) to avoid the
beam and negate the effect; otherwise, any inanimate matter up to 1"
cube (or any equivalent volume) can be instantaneously disintegrated.

##### Geas

(affects: 1 subject, duration: special, range: 3") The subject is
compelled to perform a
[quest](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#quest) specified by the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user). Should
the subject dally or deviate from his
[quest](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#quest) he will lose 1-6
points of [strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) each
day until he either dies or resumes the
[quest](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#quest). Only the completion
of the [quest](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#quest) or a
successful [dispel
evil](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-evil) (or dispel good)
will end this spell.

##### Invoke Stalker

(affects: 1 stalker, duration: special, range 1") Conjures an [invisible
stalker](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#an-invisible-stalker) from
the null-dimensions which the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can
instruct to carry out some task. The [invisible
stalker](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#an-invisible-stalker) will
perform this mission single-mindedly until the task is completed, it is
destroyed in [combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat), or is
dismissed by a [dispel
evil](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-evil). It will resent
this servitude, however, and if after any day of service the referee
throws a 12 on two six-sided
[dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-dice_1) the [invisible
stalker](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#an-invisible-stalker) will
subvert the
[magic-user’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
[intent](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intent) by observing his
orders absolutely literally to the letter. If ordered to guard a
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) hoard, for
example, it might take the hoard to its home dimension and guard it
there.

##### Move Earth

(affects: 1 body of earth, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 24") Above
ground this spell causes a hill, ridge, bluff, or similar body of earth
within range and sight to be moved. Underground it
[moves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) a
cavern, chamber, passageway, or similar feature through the ground, or
else [moves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2)
some protuberance of earth within a large cavern. The body of earth is
moved at a gentle rate of 6". Creatures, vegetation, and structures can
be carried along unharmed or structures can be undermined, at the
referee’s discretion. Alternatively, a [clay
golem](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#golems-clay) or [earth
elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals-earth) can be
driven back 12" suffering 6-36
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). Note that earth is
moved but not reshaped.

##### Project Image

(affects: 1 image, duration: 6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), range: 24") Projects
a quasi-real image of the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
anywhere within range and sight. The image is indistinguishable from the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) and is
completely under his control. He knows everything his image senses and
can direct it to perform any action he himself could perform including
[casting](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory)
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells). The
image is impervious to harm except that a successful [dispel
magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-magic) will end its
existence.
[Spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells)
originating from the image are in actuality
[cast](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory) by
the [magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) and
are erased from his memory as usual.

##### Reincarnation

(affects: 1 creature, duration: permanent, range: touch) Restores a
slain character to life in another body so long as he has not been dead
any longer than one day per level of the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user). Rising
from the dead is a great ordeal and the subject must make a successful
[shock survival](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#shock-survival)
check in order to reincarnate. Should this prove successful his body is
transformed (according to his
[alignment](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#alignment)) and he
awakes without need for recuperation.

Delving Deeper Online table1\_23

|                                  |                     |              |            |
|----------------------------------|---------------------|--------------|------------|
| Table 1.23 Reincarnation Outcome |                     |              |            |
|                                  | Subject’s Alignment |              |            |
| 1-10                             | Chaotic             | Neutral      | Lawful     |
| 1                                | Anti-cleric         | Caveman      | Cleric     |
| 2                                | Doppelganger        | Centaur      | Dryad      |
| 3                                | Fighter             | Doppelganger | Dwarf      |
| 4                                | Hobgoblin           | Dwarf        | Elf        |
| 5                                | Lizardman           | Elf          | Fighter    |
| 6                                | Magic-user          | Fighter      | Gnome      |
| 7                                | Minotaur            | Halfling     | Halfling   |
| 8                                | Ogre                | Magic-user   | Magic-user |
| 9                                | Orc                 | Pixie        | Unicorn    |
| 10                               | Wereboar            | Weretiger    | Werebear   |

The reincarnated character retains his former
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence),
[wisdom](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wisdom), and memories but
otherwise assumes all faculties of his new form. Any former spell
[casting](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory)
ability is [lost](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#becoming-lost). If
a player character [class](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#classes)
or race is indicated throw a six-sided die to determine the character’s
new level. [Elves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elves_1) may
split their levels between the fighting and magic-using (and thieving,
if
[thieves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-thief-optional-class)
are used) [classes](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#classes).
[Halflings](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#halflings_1) will have
only half as many levels as indicated. No character can advance in level
by [reincarnation](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reincarnation) in
any case.

##### Slaying Spell

(affects: 4-24 creatures, range: 24") Instantly slays 4-24 creatures
within a 7" diameter area. The spell is indiscriminate and must affect
the indicated number of creatures beginning with those nearest to the
target. No [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) is allowed but
[superheroic-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
are unaffected.

##### Stone to Flesh

([reversible](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reversible-spells),
affects: 1 creature, duration: permanent, range: 12") Restores one
petrified creature (and any possessions) to living flesh. Returning to
the flesh is a great ordeal and the subject must make a successful
[shock survival](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#shock-survival)
check or else be slain. The reverse, flesh to stone, turns one living
creature (and any possessions carried) to stone. A successful [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
petrification](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#paralysis-and-petrification)
will negate the effect.

##### Wall of Iron

(affects: 6" wall, duration: permanent, range: 6") Conjures a daunting
bulkhead of solid iron 1ft thick and up to 6" long and 20ft high (or any
equivalent dimensions). It can be plain or featured and straight or
curved, as the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
desires, including a 10ft high 4" diameter circle. It is impervious to
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) such
as [sixth sense](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#sixth-sense),
[passwall](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#passwall), and [transmute
rock to mud](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#transmute-rock-to-mud)
and is largely impenetrable to ordinary means of battery or attack. It
can be dismissed by a successful [dispel
magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-magic).

# Section II: Delving & Exploration

## Preparation for the Campaign

The referee should be comfortable with these rules and the mechanics of
play, but even then a new
[campaign](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-campaign) requires
some preparation before play can start. The referee begins by envisaging
a fantasy [world](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#creating-a-world)
in which his new
[campaign](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-campaign) will take
place. He need not etch out the entire history of the
[world](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#creating-a-world)
immediately; the merest hint of what the
[world](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#creating-a-world) might
promise is sufficient at this early stage. Next, he requires the outline
of a continent or similar region for the players to explore. Finally, he
requires a detailed map of a town or village and the countryside in
which play will begin.

The referee should familiarize himself with the geography, water
sources, and
[settlements](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#settlements-and-strongholds_1)
(human and otherwise) near to the start of play, noting any particular
detail of each. Using broad strokes rather than exacting detail will
save time and allow room for the players to influence the
[world](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#creating-a-world),
encouraging a dynamic
[campaign](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-campaign) that feels
“alive”.

After establishing the [campaign
world](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#creating-a-world) the referee
should map several
[underworld](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#underworld-exploration)
[dungeons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#populating-a-dungeon) and
stock these with
