Should a [dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) be
sleeping the characters may, if great caution is employed, approach
without waking it. If this is successfully accomplished a single
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) of
[surprise](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#surprise) attacks is
allowed at +2 to hit. These will wake the
[dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) immediately and
thereafter regular [combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat)
will ensue.

##### Dragon Breath Weapon

A [dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) can use its
dreaded [breath
weapon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) only thrice
per day and will do so to its maximum advantage. Those unfortunates that
are targeted suffer [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage)
equal to the [dragon’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons)
current [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) or
half this number with a successful [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus breath
weapons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon).

##### Dragon Magic

Should a [dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) be
magic-using it will know as many
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) as
it has [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice). It
will have access to 1st level
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) as a
hatchling, 2nd level
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) as a
young [dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons), and 3rd
level
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells)
thereafter. [Golden
dragons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons-golden) only
continue in this manner, attaining 6th level
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) as
ancient [dragons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons).

##### If Multiple Dragons

are encountered they will be related individuals of the same type. A
pair of [dragons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) could be
siblings, mother and daughter, or a mated pair as appropriate for their
age category. Hatchlings and young
[dragons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) will be the
offspring of adults present. If these are attacked, the adults will
immediately use their [breath
weapons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) against the
offender. If either adult of a mated pair is attacked, its mate will
retaliate at +4 to hit the following
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) or for the remainder
of the [combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat) if its mate
is slain.

##### Subduing Dragons

With the exception of the golden type,
[dragons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) can be
[subdued](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#attacking-to-subdue) as
usual. A
[subdued](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#attacking-to-subdue)
[dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) will serve so long
as its master remains in a commanding position but will otherwise
attempt to escape or slay him. A
[subdued](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#attacking-to-subdue)
[dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) can be sold into
servitude on the open market for 500-1,000 gp per [hit
point](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) it
has—although the player may have difficulty finding an appropriate
buyer.

##### Dragon Treasure

Hatchlings have not yet acquired any
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures). Older
[dragons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) have a hoard
worth ½ a type H
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) for each age
category beyond hatchling.

##### Dragons, Black

dwell in swamps, marshes, and jungles. They are patient hunters and can
[fly](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fly),
[swim](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#swimming), and breath
underwater indefinitely. While a black
[dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) lurks underwater
the pool will gradually stagnate and become foul. Its [breath
weapon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) is a searing
jet of acid which affects all targets in a line. They are themselves
invulnerable to acid.

##### Dragons, Blue

are found in arid regions soaring on the hot desert airs. They are
shrewd hunters and love best to drop unseen from the azure skies but can
also bury themselves in sand dunes for ambush. A blue
[dragon’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) [breath
weapon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) is a cracking
[bolt](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#arrows-and-bolts) of
lightning which will affect all targets in a line. They are themselves
invulnerable to lightning.

##### Dragons, Golden

can be found in any habitat. Despite being the only lawful
[dragons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) they will not
serve any player and cannot be
[subdued](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#attacking-to-subdue) in
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat). They are very
intelligent and always magic-using and will employ
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells)
cleverly in [combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat).
Moreover, they are highly magic resistant and make all [saving
throws](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) versus
magical attacks at +4. A gold
[dragon’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) [breath
weapon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) is a sonic
blast that will also
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) structures. They
sometimes [polymorph](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#polymorph)
into human form to
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) freely
among [men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men).

##### Dragons, Green

are found in daunting woods and impenetrable forests. They are voracious
hunters of food and
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) and keen
gatherers of intelligence. They will attack weak targets immediately but
stalk more formidable prey. A green
[dragon’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) [breath
weapon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) is a
withering cone of chlorine gas. They are immune to
[poison](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#neutralize-poison).

##### Dragons, Red

dwell in mountain caves from where they terrorize the surrounds. They
are voracious predators and their greed is legendary. They will usually
attack on sight but prefer not to destroy
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) with their
fearsome fiery [breath
weapon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) if possible.
They are themselves invulnerable to fire.

##### Dragons, White

dwell in polar regions and are cunning predators that can
[fly](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fly),
[swim](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#swimming), and tunnel through
snow and ice. They will not slip on ice and their [breath
weapon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) is a
blistering cone of cold. They are themselves invulnerable to cold.

##### Dryads

are shy and reclusive creatures who have exhaustive knowledge of their
forest homes. Each is bound to an individual tree and can go no farther
than 24" from it. A dryad is non-violent but can employ a powerful charm
causing a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell) at −2. Those who fail
will never leave the forest.

##### Dwarfs

dwell underground and see equally well by day or by night. They are
redoubtable [fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter)
and [ogres](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ogres),
[trolls](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#trolls), and
[giants](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants) score only half
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) against them. Away
from the lair a troop of dwarfs is always accompanied by one 1st-6th
level [fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) for
every 40 dwarfs. In their
[stronghold](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strongholds) lair there
will instead be one 3rd-6th level
[fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) for every 40
dwarfs. A leveled
[fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) has a 10%
chance per level of being equipped with magic
[armor](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields), a magic
[shield](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields), and a
magic [axe](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#axes) or hammer (check
separately for each). A dwarf
[stronghold](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strongholds) is 50%
likely to be additionally defended by domesticated animals such as 1-6
[bears](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#bears) or 1-8 [giant
weasels](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#weasels-giant) (check
separately for each).

##### An Efreeti

is a creature of fire and an irreconcilable enemy of the
[djinn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#a-djinni). They are
immensely strong—being able to bear what eight
[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men) can carry—and deal 2-12
[hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) in
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat). Efreet can also
[fly](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fly), become invisible, and
magically create any desired object at will. Soft materials including
food, drink, and garments are permanent. Harder materials have a shorter
existence; efreet gold lasts only a day, steel but one hour. An efreeti
can also create magical
[illusions](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#illusions) on a whim and
these are equal to the
[phantasm](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#phantasm) spell except
that an efreeti has no need to concentrate to maintain the
[illusion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#illusions). Additionally
they can cause a [wall of
fire](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wall-of-fire) to spring up and
can themselves become incendiaries. If bound into service an efreeti
will grudgingly serve for a year and a day but no longer.

### Elementals

An elemental is an essential force of nature and is one of four types:
earth, air, fire, and water. Each can appear in three sizes: 8, 12, or
16 [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice).
Elementals of any sort are affected by magical weapons only.

All elementals, no matter the [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) or
type, must be controlled by the summoner. If the summoner’s
concentration is broken for any reason the elemental will cease whatever
it is doing,
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) at its
best [speed](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#speed), and attempt to
kill him. Anyone between the elemental and its summoner will be attacked
and everyone else will be ignored. Once control has been relinquished
there is no way to regain it. The elemental will attack until it or its
target is destroyed and immediately return to its home dimension.

##### Elementals, Air

The only means of motility possessed by an air
[elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals) is flight
but they have absolute control over their
[movement](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2),
hovering or changing [speed](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#speed)
at will. These
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2) cause 2-7
[hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) and attack at +2 to
hit versus
[aerial](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#aerial-exploration)
opponents. They can spin into a fearsome whirlwind 3" wide at the base,
6" wide at the apex, and 1" of height for each [hit
die](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#hit-dice) possessed (e.g., 8"
tall for an 8 HD air
[elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals)). The
whirlwind takes a [turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) to
form and another to dissipate and will sweep away all
[normal-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types).

##### Elementals, Earth

These creatures of earth and stone will strike with their mighty fists
for 3-18 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) to opponents
standing on solid ground and causing structural
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) to constructions
such as castle walls. Against opponents not standing on solid ground an
earth [elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals)
inflicts 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). Earth
[elementals](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals)
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) at 6"
over or through earth but cannot cross water. A [move
earth](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#move-earth) spell will drive
an earth [elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals)
back 12" and cause 6-36 points of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage).

##### Elementals, Fire

Fire [elementals](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals)
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) 12" per
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) but cannot cross
water. The touch of these
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2) causes
inflammable materials to ignite. In
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat) a fire
[elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals) usually
causes 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). Against other
fire-based creatures ([red
dragons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons-red),
[salamanders](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#salamanders), [fire
giants](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants-fire), and so on)
they cause only 2-7 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). Fire
[elementals](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals) can only be
summoned from a large source of heat such as a bonfire, a furnace, or
molten lava.

##### Elementals, Water

Water [elementals](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals) are
very dangerous in their environment, causing 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) in the water but
only 1-6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) on dry land. They
can overturn boats and small
[vessels](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#oared-vessels) and prevent
large [vessels](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#oared-vessels) from
moving. Water
[elementals](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals) can only be
summoned from a large body of water such as a stream, pond, or lake.
Once formed, a water
[elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals) must remain
within 6" of a large body of water. Its [movement
rate](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#movement-rates_1) is 18" in
water but 6" out of water.

##### Elves

are reclusive woodland folk. They can
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) silently
and almost invisibly through woods in their gray-green cloaks and are
equipped with swords and
[spears](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spears) or swords and
[bows](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#bows) (50% chance of either).
For every 40 elves encountered there will be a leader-type with 2-4
[fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) levels and
2-6 [magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
levels. For every 80 elves encountered there will be an additional
4th/6th level
[fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter)/[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user).
Leader-types may possess magic items as per
[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men). All elves add +1 [hit
point](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) when employing
magic weapons and those with
[bows](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#bows) can
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) and fire
without penalty.

##### Fish, Giant

are of various sorts including barracuda, gar, and pike. They are
aggressive hunters and always hungry. They occur in wild schools and as
domesticated guardians around
[merman](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#mermen) and
[nixie](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#nixies) lairs.

##### Gargoyles

appear much as the sculptural depictions in gothic architecture. They
can remain perfectly still indefinitely and are indistinguishable from
ordinary statues when so perched. They are notoriously hostile, however,
and will attack without provocation 75% of the time. They are fond of
ambush and [normal
weapons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-weapons) do them no
harm.

##### A Gelatinous Cube

is a cube-shaped, transparent scavenger that shapes itself to fit
[dungeon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#populating-a-dungeon)
corridors up to 10ft by 10ft wide and
[moves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) about
sweeping them clean. It picks up and absorbs everything from rocks and
carrion to living things and
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures), which it is
unable to digest. Thus, these scavengers carry a miscellany of durable
items (coins, gems,
[daggers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#daggers),
[helms](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magical-helms), and so on)
suspended in their transparent innards. Contact with a gelatinous cube
causes paralysis unless a successful [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) is made, and
thereafter causes 1-6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) per
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) as the flesh is
digested. They are invulnerable to cold and lightning, and immune to
[fear](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fear), paralysis, and
[polymorph](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#polymorph).

##### Ghouls

are eaters of living and carrion flesh. Their attack rolls and
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
checks are penalized by −2 in daylight but the touch of these undead
creatures causes paralysis for 1
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) in
[normal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types)
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) (except
[elves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elves_1), who are immune). A
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) slain by a
ghoul will arise again the following night as a ghoul.

### Giants

Giants are enormous, ugly humanoids who can hurl great rocks 20" for
2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) and need never
check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
against [man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types).
Unless noted otherwise, giants also cause 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) in
[melee](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#melee_2)
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat). A wandering giant
carries a great shoulder sack that contains his possessions including
rocks, prisoners, other miscellany, and 1,000-6,000 gp worth of coins.
Giant lairs are 50% likely to be guarded by a 5-10 headed
[hydra](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#hydras) (with a throw of 1-4
on a six-sided die), or 2-20
[wolves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wolves) (with a throw of
5), or 1-6 [bears](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#bears) (with a
throw of 6). Giants are of various sorts including:

##### Giants, Cloud

are 18ft tall and inhabit unbelievable castles among the clouds. They
cause 3-18 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) in
[melee](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#melee_2)
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat) and their sense of
smell is so amazingly keen that they are rarely surprised.

##### Giants, Fire

are 12ft tall and of stocky build. They cause 4-14 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) in
[melee](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#melee_2)
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat) and lair in castles
and caverns wherever there is lava, fire, or great heat. They are
themselves invulnerable to fire.

##### Giants, Frost

are 16ft tall and cause 3-13 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) in
[melee](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#melee_2)
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat). They favor huge
horned [helmets](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magical-helms) and
lair in frigid castles and caverns. They are themselves invulnerable to
cold.

##### Giants, Hill

are the most base sort. They are 12ft tall and lair in rudimentary
caves. They frequently associate with
[ogres](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ogres),
[orcs](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#orcs), and other wicked
creatures.

##### Giants, Stone

are 14ft tall and inhabit isolated mountain cavern systems. They hurl
rocks for 3-18 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage).

##### Giants, Storm

are 20ft tall and cause 6-21 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) in
[melee](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#melee_2)
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat). They inhabit
formidable castles situated in out of the way places including islands,
mountains, and cloud tops. They are able to [control
weather](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#control-weather) to create
stormy conditions—which they will do when angry or expecting battle. As
well as hurling rocks a
[storm](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#storms_1)
[giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants) can call down a
lightning strike for 8-48 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) in thunderstorm
conditions. They are themselves invulnerable to lightning.

##### Gnolls

fight with +2
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks).
The lair will contain a chieftain and 1-6 bodyguards who fight as 4 and
3 [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice)
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2),
respectively.

##### Gnomes

are found in Arctic climes. They are smaller and more reclusive than
their cousins, the
[dwarfs](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dwarfs_1), but have longer
beards and bigger noses.

##### Goblins

are small, malicious humanoids who operate underground or at night,
adjusting attack and
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
checks by −1 in full daylight. Each fighting goblin carries coins worth
1-6 gp with him, even outside the lair. The lair will be a cave complex
containing as many non-combatants as combatants, as well as a goblin
king and 4-24 bodyguards who fight as 2 and 1+1 [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice)
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2),
respectively. The lair is 50% likely to contain an additional 3-12
[giant wolves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wolves-giant) and
3-18 [ogres](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ogres) (check
separately for each).

### Golems

Golems are powerful automatons created by high level
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) and
[clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) that exist
only to obey the commands of their creators, following instructions to
the letter. They are ponderous and dull-witted but incredibly strong. In
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat) they strike for
2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) and can batter
through wooden structures including
[doors](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#doors). They are largely
invulnerable to harmful magic, but there is a 1% chance per
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) of
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat) that a golem will
go berserk. Should this occur the creator cannot regain control and the
golem will continue to attack whatever creature harms it or is nearest
until it is destroyed.

##### Golems, Clay

are created by high level
[clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) from blood and
pliable clay. A
[disintegrate](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#disintegrate) spell
will [slow](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#slow) a clay
[golem](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#golems) and cause 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) and a [move
earth](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#move-earth) spell will drive
a clay [golem](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#golems) back 12" and
cause 6-36 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage); otherwise, they
can only be harmed by magical weapons. After one
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) of
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat) a clay
[golem](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#golems) comes under the
influence of a [haste](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#haste) spell
for the next three [turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).
Injuries caused by a clay
[golem](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#golems) cannot be cured by a
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) lower than 9th
level.

##### Golems, Flesh

are powerful automatons created by high level
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) from
stitched together body parts, but they are not undead. Cold and fire
based
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) will
[slow](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#slow) a flesh
[golem](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#golems) and lightning will
[heal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#healing) it; otherwise, they
can only be harmed by magical weapons.

##### Gorgons

are aggressive, bull-like creatures covered in iron
[scales](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#scale) with a rightly
feared [breath
weapon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) that turns
targets to stone. The [breath
weapon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) extends to a
6" long by 2" wide cone and is usable thrice per day.

##### Gothrogs

are [giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants), fiery fiends of
dreadful power and
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence). They
see in darkness as [men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men) see in
daylight and combust inflammable materials by merely passing nearby.
Fire and [normal
weapons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-weapons) cannot harm
them and it is 75% likely that magic
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) will
not affect them.

Gothrogs carry great, flaming, [magic
swords](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magic-swords) and fiery
whips and can attack with either or both each
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns). Should a gothrog
employ both weapons it can target two opponents, causing 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) to each. If it
employs only one weapon it does so at +2 to hit. The flaming sword
causes 3-18 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). The whip causes
only 1-6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage), but entangles the
target so the gothrog can drag him unto itself, where upon it will
immolate and cause an additional 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) to everybody within
1".

Gothrogs need never check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
and cannot be
[subdued](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#attacking-to-subdue). A
powerful chaotic character might attempt to
[enlist](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#enlisting-monsters) one
with a substantial offering, but only a top level
[anti-cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-anti-cleric) has
the presence necessary to
[keep](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#keep) a gothrog firmly under
control. A gothrog would ever be bent upon usurping the authority of any
other master.

##### Gray Ooze

is a creeping
[dungeon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#populating-a-dungeon)
scavenger which is difficult to spot in dim
[light](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#light_2) as it appears much
like wet stonework. It can
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) along
walls, floors, and ceilings equally and can squeeze through tiny
openings including cracks in stonework and under
[doors](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#doors). It dissolves metal
[armor](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields) in one
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) and causes 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) per
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) to flesh but has no
effect on wood or stone. It is impervious to cold and fire but subject
to lightning and [normal
weaponry](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-weapons) (but note
its effect on metal).

##### Green Slime

is a pernicious
[dungeon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#populating-a-dungeon)
hazard that clings to walls, floors, and ceilings. It begins to eat
through flesh, wood, and metal (but not stone) after one
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) of contact,
transmuting these into green slime. It cannot be physically scraped off
so anything it comes into contact with must be discarded immediately. It
is impervious to lightning and physical blows but is harmed by cold and
fire. A [remove
disease](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#remove-disease) spell will
slay it instantly.

##### Griffons

are majestic creatures with the forequarters of an eagle and the
hindquarters of a [lion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#lions).
They are fleet and fiercely territorial and will attack without
provocation should anything approach the aerie lair. Griffons make loyal
steeds if they can be trained but crave
[horse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#horses) flesh above other
foods and will attack any
[horse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#horses) or
[pegasi](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#pegasi) within 36".

##### Halflings

are small, peaceful folk interested chiefly in home comforts. When the
need arises they are able to
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) silently
and almost invisibly and to hide quite superbly. For every 30 halflings
encountered there will be a leader with 1-4
[fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) levels. All
halflings are deadly accurate with hurled
[missiles](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#missile-fire) adjusting
attack rolls by +3.

##### Hippogriffs

are admirable beasts with the forequarters of an eagle and the
hindquarters of a [horse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#horses).
They are omnivorous hunters and highly sought as mounts for their great
[speed](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#speed)—despite their
intolerance of [pegasi](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#pegasi).
They need never check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
when defending their nest.

##### Hobgoblins

are the largest and most fearless
[goblins](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#goblins). They are
armored, well organized, and have +1 to
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
checks except in full daylight where they must instead adjust attack
rolls by −1. Wandering bands are always led by a sergeant who fights as
a 2 [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice)
[monster](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2).

The lair will be a village, ruin, or cave complex containing half as
many non-combatants as combatants as well as a hobgoblin king and 2-12
bodyguards who fight as 3 and 2 [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice)
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2),
respectively. The lair is 50% likely to contain an additional 3-12
[giant wolves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wolves-giant), 3-18
[ogres](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ogres), and 2-12
[trolls](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#trolls) (check separately
for each).

##### Horses

are domesticated riding animals and beasts of burden. Riding horses,
draft horses, and mules will flee fire and may be panicked by strange
smells. Only warhorses and destriers will attack in
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat), having a single
attack roll even versus
[normal-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types).

Only [mules](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#horses) are agile
enough to enter the labyrinthine passages of a
[dungeon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#populating-a-dungeon).

##### Hydras

are large reptilian
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2) with one head
per [hit die](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#hit-dice). Each
serpentine head can be destroyed by sustaining 6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). The entirety of
the beast is slain only when all of its individual heads are dispatched.
Circumstances allowing, each head can select an individual target and
make an attack roll each
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns). However, it attacks
as a [fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) rather
than as a [monster](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2).

##### An Invisible Stalker

is a creature from the null-dimensions which can be conjured to the
material [world](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#creating-a-world)
by powerful magic. It is indistinguishable from air without the benefit
of a [detect
invisibility](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#detect-invisibility)
or a [true seeing](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#true-seeing)
spell. It is a faultless tracker and, if encountered in the material
[world](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#creating-a-world), an
invisible stalker will be single-mindedly preoccupied with whatever
mission it is carrying out.

##### A Juggernaut

is an incredibly massive creature of solid ore, though whether it is
self-willed or magically motivated is unknown. These behemoths have only
ever been sighted individually and can take any form; a great armored
knight, a mammoth, and a rhinoceros have all been reported. A juggernaut
is so massive that it is impelled upon huge stone rollers with anything
falling in its path being crushed utterly beneath it.

Regardless of its form a juggernaut always has a massive dark jewel
affixed to it; between the eyes, in the chest, or atop a
[helm](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magical-helms),
[staff](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands), or sword,
and so on. The jewel glows with an eerie
[light](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#light_2) and can
[cast](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory)
out a [slaying spell](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#slaying-spell)
each [turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) or an improved
[hold person](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#hold-person) spell
which will affect 2-12
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) who save at
−2 or a single [man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types)
who saves at −6. Unfortunates so held will soon be crushed beneath the
juggernaut. If the jewel is somehow removed from a juggernaut it has no
magical properties but is worth 20,000-120,000 gp.

If it comes to blows a juggernaut deals a crushing 5-30 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). It is impervious
to most magical attacks and can only be harmed by magical weapons of +3
or better quality. A juggernaut need never check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
and cannot be
[subdued](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#attacking-to-subdue).

##### Kobolds

are small, cowardly, reptilian humanoids who dwell in quags and
wetlands. They are able swimmers and prefer to attack in great numbers
from ambush. Each fighting kobold carries coins worth 1-6 gp with him,
even outside the lair. Their lair will be a marshy cave complex
containing as many non-combatants as combatants as well as a kobold king
and 5-30 bodyguards who fight as 1+1 and 1 [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice)
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2),
respectively. The lair is 50% likely to contain an additional 3-24
[crocodiles](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#crocodiles) and 2-12
[giant
lizards](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#lizards-giant-and-large)
(check separately for each). Their
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
checks are adjusted by −1 unless they are defending their lair and they
outnumber their enemies by 3 to 1 or more.

##### Leeches, Giant

are loathsome swamp parasites that will attach to victims on a
successful attack and drain one experience level in the
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) after attachment and
another every other [turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)
thereafter until either the victim or the leech is slain.

##### Lions

are the great cats of the plains. They occur in hot to tropical climates
and are territorial hunters who will stalk prey patiently in order to
attack by [surprise](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#surprise). They
can leap 30ft forward but dislike climbing and
[swimming](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#swimming). They cause 2-7
[hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) or, if an attack
roll exceeds the number required to hit by 4 or more or is a 20 in any
case, 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage).

##### Lions, Spotted

are similar to regular
[lions](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#lions) except that they are
larger and occur in caves and mountainous regions. They cause 3-8 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) or, if an attack
roll exceeds the number required to hit by 4 or more or is a 20 in any
case, 4-14 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage).

### Living Statues

Living statues are large, powerful humanoid automatons. Standing
silently they are indistinguishable from ordinary statues of great size.
Living statues are extremely heavy and
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2)
ponderously but with purpose. They can batter through wooden structures,
including [doors](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#doors), and are
largely invulnerable to harmful magic.

##### Living Statues, Iron

are
[cast](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory)
from solid metal. In
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat) they can exhale a
1" radius cloud of
[poisonous](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#poison) gas or else
strike for 4-24 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). Lightning attacks
will [slow](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#slow) them and fire will
[heal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#healing) them; otherwise,
they can only be harmed by magical weapons of +3 or better quality.

##### Living Statues, Stone

are hewn from solid rock. In
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat) they can
[slow](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#slow) one target per
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) or else strike for
3-18 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). Cold and fire will
[slow](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#slow) them and [stone to
flesh](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#stone-to-flesh) will
[heal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#healing) them; otherwise,
they can only be harmed by magic which specifically affects stone or
magical weapons of +2 or better quality.

##### Lizards, Giant and Large

are found in desert and jungle climes. Large lizards can be up to 6ft in
length and [giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants) lizards
up to 15ft. Both types have superb camouflage markings and can hold an
absolutely still position indefinitely. If a
[giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants) lizard should throw
an attack roll of 20, its bite will clamp onto its prey and not let go,
automatically causing
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) each
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) thereafter until
either it or its prey is slain.

##### Lizardmen

are reptilian humanoids with
[crocodile](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#crocodiles)-like jaws
and tails and a rudimentary
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence). They
employ primitive [spears](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spears)
and clubs and will capture as many humans as possible—returning with
them to their lair for a tribal feast.

The lair will be a wet or marshy cave complex containing half as many
non-combatants as combatants as well as an equal number of
[kobolds](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#kobolds) and 2-16
prisoners. There will be a lizardman chieftain and 1-6 bodyguards who
fight as 4 and 3 [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice)
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2),
respectively. There is also a 33% chance that the lair will contain 2-12
[giant
lizards](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#lizards-giant-and-large),
3-24 [crocodiles](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#crocodiles), or a
[dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) (check for each
separately). If a [dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons)
is present it will be an adult, mature, or old specimen of the black or
green type.

##### Lycanthropes

are also known as werebeasts and are of various sorts. All are
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) afflicted
with lycanthropy and cannot be harmed by [normal
weaponry](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-weapons) unless it
is silvered. Any
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) seriously
wounded by a lycanthrope will become one of the same type at the next
full moon unless he receives a [remove
disease](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#remove-disease) spell
before this occurs.

Outside the lair werebeasts run in packs of 1-10 adults. If more than 8
are encountered in the lair one-third will be adults with the remainder
being non-combative young. A lair will also contain animals of the
appropriate type (1-6 [bears](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#bears)
for werebears, 1-12 [boars](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#boars)
for wereboars, 1-6 [tigers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#tigers)
for weretigers, or 1-10
[wolves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wolves) for werewolves). If
the young are attacked adult females will retaliate at +4 to hit for the
remainder of the [combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat).
If females are attacked the adult males will retaliate at +4 to hit
thereafter. If all adults are slain the young are automatically
[subdued](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#attacking-to-subdue).

##### Manticoras

are great [lion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#lions)-like beasts
with [dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons)-wings,
[man](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men)-like faces, and powerful
tails that culminate in 24 iron spikes which can be flung in a volley of
6 at any target within 18". These are carnivorous and favor human flesh.

##### Mastodons

are proto-elephants encountered on open plains in any climate. They
occur in herds and are generally non-aggressive unless threatened or in
the mating season. At these times the males will attack anyone who might
dare to approach the herd. They cause 4-14 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) due to their
prodigious size.

##### Medusae

have the lower body of a great serpent and the upper body of a woman,
except that their hair is a tangle of deadly venomous
[snakes](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#snakes-giant-and-large). So
abhorrent is a medusa’s appearance that anyone who meets its gaze will
be turned to stone unless he makes a successful [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
petrification](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#paralysis-and-petrification).
Any medusa who sees her own refection will likewise be turned to stone.

### Men

Men are of various sorts and lair in villages, caves, hide-outs,
encampments, and so on.
[Brigand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men-brigands) and
[buccaneer](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men-buccaneers) lairs
will have 2-12 prisoners who will always be persons of some importance.
[Bandit](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men-bandits) and
[pirate](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men-pirates) lairs will
have 3-30 prisoners of any sort. A
[nomad](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men-nomads) encampment is
always guarded by an additional 20-40
[nomads](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men-nomads) on foot.

Each individual man will have 2-12 sp on his person (in addition to
whatever [treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) may
be found in the lair) except that
[pirates](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men-pirates) and
[buccaneers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men-buccaneers) have
2-12 gp each instead. For every 25, 50, and 100 men encountered there
will be an additional leader who is a 3rd-4th, 5th-6th, or 7th-8th level
[fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter),
respectively. If at least 200 men are encountered it is 50% likely they
are also accompanied by a 5th-8th level
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) and a
3rd-6th level [cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric)
(check separately for each). If 300 men are encountered there absolutely
will be an additional 9th-12th level
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) and an
additional 7th-10th level
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric).

Leader-types have a chance of possessing magical items appropriate to
their [class](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#classes).
[Fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) have a 10%
chance per experience level of possessing a [magic
sword](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magic-swords) and are half as
likely to possess a magic
[shield](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields) or magic
[armor](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields).
[Clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) are 2% likely
per experience level to possess a magic
[mace](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#flails-and-maces),
[flail](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#flails-and-maces), hammer,
or [staff](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) and are
5% likely to possess a magic
[shield](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields) or magic
[armor](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields).
[Magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) are 5%
likely per experience level to possess a magic
[wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) and are
equally likely to possess a magic
[ring](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings) or a [miscellaneous
magic
item](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#miscellaneous-magic-items).
Check separately for each item in all cases.

##### Men, Bandits

are desperate and surly scavengers equipped simply with clubs,
[daggers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#daggers), or
[axes](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#axes), and
[shields](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields).

##### Men, Berserkers

are warriors maddened with battle lust. They attack at +2 to hit [versus
man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#versus-man-types) and
need never check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks).
They carry two-handed weapons but wear no
[armor](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields). Their
leader-types are exclusively
[fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter).

##### Men, Brigands

are well-organized robbers and highway
[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men). They wear leather
[armor](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields), carry
[shields](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields), are
armed with swords, [axes](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#axes),
[maces](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#flails-and-maces), short
[bows](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#bows), or
[spears](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spears) and have a +1
adjustment to
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
checks.

##### Men, Buccaneers

are picaroons and castaways who ply the shores for easy pickings from
skiffs and pickets. They are unarmored and quick and carry swords or
clubs and [daggers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#daggers) as a
main gauche.

##### Men, Dervishes

are religious fanatics of the lawful sort. They attack at +2 to hit
[versus man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#versus-man-types)
and need never check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
due to their fanaticism. They carry clerical weaponry and
[shields](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields) and
their leader-types are exclusively
[clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric).

##### Men, Mercenaries

are professional sell-swords and soldiers of fortune. They are well
organized but untrustworthy military
[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men) possibly open to offers
of employment. They typically have leather
[armor](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields),
[helmets](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magical-helms), and
[shields](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields) and are
armed with swords, [spears](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spears),
pole arms, or crossbows. With a throw of 5-6 on a six-sided die
one-third of their force will also be
[mounted](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#mounted-combat).

##### Men, Nomads

are desert or steppe raiders who are always
[mounted](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#mounted-combat). They
carry short [bows](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#bows),
[spears](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spears), and
[shields](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields).

##### Men, Pirates

are ruthless sea [dogs](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dogs) and
cut throats who pillage waterways and coastal regions from their sloops
and galleys. They are unarmored and quick and arm themselves with curved
swords or clubs and
[daggers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#daggers) as a main-gauche.
They have a +1 adjustment to
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
checks.

##### Men, Zealots

are religious fanatics of the chaotic sort. They attack at +2 to hit
[versus man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#versus-man-types)
and need never check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
due to their fanaticism. They carry clerical weaponry and
[shields](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields) and
their leader-types are exclusively
[anti-clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-anti-cleric).

##### Mermen

are aquatic warriors. Against
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) in the sea
they attack at +2 and need never check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks).
They can remain underwater indefinitely and are only subject to
[missile](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#missile-fire) fire if they
rise to the surface, which they must do to grapple or board ships. On
land or aboard ships they suffer a −2 penalty to attack rolls and
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
checks. Their scaly skin is equal to leather
[armor](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields) and they
fight with [spears](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spears) and
[daggers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#daggers). Meremen have
leader-types as do [men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men)
although these are exclusively
[fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter).

##### Minotaurs

are great bull-headed humanoids half again as large as a
[man](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men). They are carnivorous
[man](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men)-eaters and will always
attack. They need never check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
and will never give up a chase so long as the prey is in sight.

##### Mummies

are invulnerable to [normal
weaponry](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-weapons) and even
magical weaponry causes them only half
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). They are
vulnerable to fire, however, even the ordinary sort. A hit from a mummy
will cause a terrible necrosis such that wounds take 10 times as long to
[heal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#healing). The first and
second applications of a [remove
disease](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#remove-disease) spell will
reduce this to 5 times and 2 times, respectively, and only a third
application will lift the affliction entirely.

##### Nixies

are small and comely fresh water sprites who are not evil but will
compel intruders to serve their needs. Any 10 nixies can jointly
[enchant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#enchanting-magic-items) a
target with a [charm
person](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#charm-person) and a water
breathing spell. A character who fails to save [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell) will immediately
proceed to the underwater lair and remain there in servitude. After a
period of one year he will return to the surface unharmed. A [dispel
magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-magic) can prematurely
break the enchantment but always has a 25% chance of failure.

Nixies arm themselves with
[daggers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#daggers) and javelins.
Their lair will be an underwater enclave containing 2-16 charmed
prisoners of various sorts, and protected by 20-120 [giant
fish](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fish-giant) such as gar or
pike. These will obey nixies but can be held at bay by any fire that
will burn underwater. Any group of 40 or more nixies can attempt to
grapple a surface ship.

##### An Ochre Jelly

is a monstrous amoeba that lives as a
[dungeon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#populating-a-dungeon)
scavenger. It is susceptible to cold and fire but lightning and weaponry
will merely divide it into two smaller parts without causing it harm. An
ochre jelly will dissolve a wooden
[shield](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields) or
[door](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#doors) in a single
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns). Flesh contacted
suffers 1-6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) per
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) but stone and metal
are impervious. It can
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) along a
wall, floor, or ceiling equally and can squeeze through tiny openings
including cracks in stonework and under
[doors](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#doors).

##### Octopi, Giant

are intelligent and lair in shipwrecks and caves preying on passing
swimmers and ships. They can grapple and capsize smaller
[vessels](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#oared-vessels) or else
make 1-6 attack rolls each
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) versus
[heroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types)/[superheroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
enemies with their stinging tentacles. They have no bones and can
squeeze through very small gaps.

##### Ogres

are thick-necked, ugly brutes half again as large as a
[man](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men) and possess great
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) but limited
wit. They cause 3-8 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) in
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat) due to their size
and [strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength). They are
so suspicious of their fellows that little
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) is left
unguarded. Instead, each ogre carries 100-600 gp with him even outside
of the lair.

##### Orcs

are fecund humanoids occurring in warlike tribes. They dislike bright
[light](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#light_2) and adjust attack
and
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
checks by −1 from in full daylight. Hostilities among orc tribes are
just as common as with neighbors of other sorts and they will attack
foreign orcs unless restrained by a strong leader. They need not check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
while they are defending their lair and they outnumber their enemies by
at least 3 to 1.

An orc lair will be either a guarded cave complex or a village protected
by a stockade and possibly an encircling
[ditch](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ditch) or moat. The lair
will contain half as many non-combatants as combatants as well as an orc
chieftain and 3-18 bodyguards who fight as 3 and 2 [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice)
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2),
respectively.

A village is 33% likely to contain an additional 1-4 catapults, a high
watch tower, 1-8 [ogres](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ogres), a
7th-8th level
[fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter), and a
9th-12th level
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) (check
for each separately). A cave complex is 33% likely to contain additional
dead [falls](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#falling) and other
[traps](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#tricks-and-traps), 1-8
[ogres](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ogres), 1-6
[trolls](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#trolls), or a
[dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) (check for each
separately). If a [dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons)
is present it will be a young, adult, or mature specimen of the black,
green, blue, or red sort.

##### Pegasi

are shy, wild, and noble winged
[horses](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#horses). If captured they
are difficult to tame and will not tolerate
[hippogriffs](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#hippogriffs) or
griffins. They will never serve chaotic characters.

##### Pixies

are small air sprites who are permanently invisible unless they desire
to be seen. They are not evil but dislike intrusion and any 10 pixies
can jointly cause a [sleep](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#sleep)
spell once per day which they use to dissuade potential offenders. They
arm themselves with
[daggers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#daggers) and short
[bows](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#bows) and always attack by
[surprise](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#surprise) unless they are
detected by magical means. Note that
[fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) of 8th level
and above will sense pixies within 3" even without seeing them.

##### Purple Worms

are voracious burrowers up to 6ft in diameter and 60ft in length that
occur almost everywhere. They always attack and need never check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks).
A purple worm causes 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) and has a deadly
venomous stringer in the tail but the huge maw is the main weapon; if a
bite attack roll exceeds the number required to hit by 4 or more, or is
a 20 in any case, a [man](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men)-sized
or smaller target will be swallowed whole. Swallowed targets will be
unconscious within 3 [turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns),
slain within 6 [turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), and
the body unrecoverable after 12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns). The interior gullet
is AC 9 but can be attacked only by
[dagger](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#daggers) or knife; at least
12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) must be caused to
cut a way out.

##### Rats, Giant

occur in plague proportions underground, squeezing through tiny gaps and
tunnels in the earth and stone work. They cause only 1-3 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) but any hit can
transmit a debilitating disease to
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) who fail to
save [versus poison](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#poison) at +4
on the die (a single [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) being required
per
[encounter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wilderness-encounters)).
Unless commanded to fight by a
[vampire](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#vampires) or
[lycanthrope](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#lycanthropes) they
have −2
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
and will flee from fire.

##### Robots

are complex metal automatons with unfathomable electronic brains. They
are self motivating and semi-intelligent and can be negotiated with to
some extent. They are usually set on a “program” from which they will
never waiver. Robots are cruelly strong and will strike for 3-8 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). Many can
[fly](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fly) by one means or another
and the remainder are equipped with a disintegration ray which can be
fired up to 6" thrice per day. A successful [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
wands](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wands-and-rays) is required
to avoid the beam. Robots cannot be
[subdued](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#attacking-to-subdue) and
need never check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks).

##### Rocs

are gargantuan raptors that prey on cattle,
[horses](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#horses), and even
elephants. Their eyesight is peerless and they always spot hidden (but
not invisible)
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types), even from
high altitude. The largest rocs are so fearsome that
[normal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types)
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) must check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
if attacked. Rocs lair in remote, mountainous aeries that are difficult
to approach except on the wing. Those found in the lair will be of mixed
life stages and there is a 50% chance that there will also be 1-6
unhatched eggs or fledglings.

Eggs and fledglings can be trained to serve as mounts if they can be
captured. If the nest contains these, the mature
[rocs](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rocs) will attack anyone who
approaches and never check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks);
otherwise, the mature [rocs](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rocs)
will tolerate lawful characters and possibly even help them. Chaotic
sorts can expect only a hostile
[reaction](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks).

##### Sabre Toothed Tigers

are the great cats of the Pliocene epoch, capable of hunting down
[dinosaurs](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dinosaurs). They are
half as large again as ordinary
[tigers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#tigers) and every bit as
canny and agile. They cause 2-9 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) or, if an attack
roll exceeds the number required to hit by 4 or more or is a 20 in any
case, 4-14 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage).

##### Salamanders

are fire-types possessing high
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence), the
upper body of a [man](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men), and the
hind section of a great serpent. They employ
[spears](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spears) and pole arms and
can be found in lava fields and environs of intense heat. Their touch
causes inflammables to combust and 1-6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) to non-fire
creatures. In [melee](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#melee_2)
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat) the upper body is
AC 5 while the serpent section is AC 3. Opponents who are not fire-types
suffer an additional 1-6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) with each hit.
However, if an attack roll exceeds the number required to hit by 4 or
more, a salamander instead constricts with its burning tail for 2-12
[hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) (plus 1-6
additional [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) to
non-fire creatures). They are themselves invulnerable to fire and
[normal weaponry](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-weapons).

##### Scorpions, Giant

are extremely aggressive hunters of
[horse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#horses)-sized proportions.
They sense things mainly through vibration in the earth and will always
attack anything that approaches. An attack roll that exceeds the number
required to hit by 4 or more, or is a 20 in any case, indicates a hit by
the venomous stinger, which is fatal unless a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
poison](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#poison) is successful;
otherwise, it is assumed to be a pincer attack that deals 3-8 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage).

##### Sea Monsters

include the largest sea serpents, the whale-like leviathan (which has
reportedly been mistaken for an island), and the many-tentacled kraken
(which is confined to a null dimension unless it is called forth by an
evil high priest to devour shipping and seaports). These exist
principally as deadly perils to be avoided.

If the players insist on rousing sea
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2) to
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat), sea serpents will
cause 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) and swallow
[man](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men)-sized or smaller targets
whole as per [purple
worms](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#purple-worms) and can
encircle longboats and smaller ships within their coils and destroy them
in 1-6 [turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns). The kraken
can capsize any ship in 1-2
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) or else deliver 1-6
attack rolls versus
[heroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types)/[superheroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
enemies, each dealing 3-18 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). The leviathan can
capsize 1-3 ships in near proximity in a single
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) or swallow a single
ship whole in its vast maw—destroying the
[vessel](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#oared-vessels) and
delivering 4-24 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) to everyone aboard
as it swallows them.

##### Shadows

are bleak incorporeal spirits that hunger for the life energy of living
things and drain 1-4 points of
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) on a hit. They
are impervious to [normal
weaponry](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-weapons) unless it
is silvered, but magical weapons will do them double
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). Any
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) reduced to nil
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) by a shadow is
slain and will arise on the following night as a shadow.
[Strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength)
[lost](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#becoming-lost) is otherwise
recovered at 1 point per hour.

##### Skeletons

are mindless undead brought forth by a
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) or
[anti-cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-anti-cleric) to
serve some wicked purpose. These can carry
[shields](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields) or wear
[armor](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields), or both,
which would improve AC to 7 or 6, respectively. They are unaffected by
[normal missiles](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-missiles),
require no sustenance, and need never check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks).

##### Snakes, Giant and Large

are encountered almost anywhere. Large snakes are up to 10ft long but
are generally non-aggressive unless hunting or provoked; they are 50%
likely to be venomous.
[Giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants) snakes are more
aggressive and are of two sorts: vipers and constrictors. Vipers slither
silently and are deadly venomous. Constrictors are non-venomous and
their bite bite deals only 1-2 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). However, if
attacking by [surprise](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#surprise) or
an attack roll exceeds the number required to hit by 4 or more, a
constrictor instead encircles its target, crushing
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) for 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) per
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns). Constrictor-types can
also be encountered at sea and are capable of encircling and destroying
small boats within their coils in 1-6
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### Spectres

are malevolent, incorporeal spirits. They can
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) through
walls, ceilings, and floors and are impervious to [normal
weaponry](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-weapons). Their
attack is a withering grasp that drains two experience levels on a hit.
A [man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) slain by a
spectre will arise the following night as a spectre under the control of
the [monster](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2) that
destroyed him. Any additional spectres encountered will be thralls of
this sort.

##### Spiders, Giant and Large

occur commonly in
[dungeons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#populating-a-dungeon).
Large spiders are the size of a
[man’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men) hand and can scurry
over floors, walls, and ceilings equally. Their bite is venomous but a
[saving throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws)
[versus poison](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#poison) is allowed
at +2. [Giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants) spiders are
true horrors up to
[horse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#horses)-sized. Their bite is
deadly venomous and they are
[web](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#web) builders—these being
equal to a [web](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#web) spell in
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength). They prefer to
wait patiently in ambush and attack unwary victims. They will flee to a
dark retreat if faced by superior opposition.

##### Squid, Giant

are voracious deep sea predators who will occasionally come to the
surface to grapple and capsize passing
[vessels](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#oared-vessels). They make
1-6 attack rolls each [turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)
against
[heroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types)/[superheroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
enemies with their numerous tentacles. If seriously challenged they can
expel a cloud of black ink and flee backwards at triple pace for three
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### Tigers

are great cats that occur in frigid to tropical woodlands. They are
canny, agile, and superb hunters who will stalk prey patiently in order
to attack by [surprise](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#surprise).
They can climb and [swim](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#swimming)
and can leap 10ft upward or 40ft forward. They cause 2-7 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) or, if an attack
roll exceeds the number required to hit by 4 or more or is a 20 in any
case, 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage).

##### Thulls

are frightful humanoids similar to feral
[hobgoblins](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#hobgoblins) in
appearance but they are far more dangerous. A thull will regenerate 1
[lost hit
point](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) at
the beginning of each [turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)
and a scratch from its black nails will cause paralysis for 1
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) in
[normal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types)
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) (except
[elves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elves_1) who are immune).

##### Titanotheres

are enormous herbivores that roam temperate plains and wetlands in
herds. Normally peaceful, they will charge and trample anything that
provokes them causing 3-18 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) due to their great
size.

##### A Titan

is a most handsome and civilized
[giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants). They are at least
as intelligent as [men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men), thrice
as tall, and incredibly strong. They deliver 6-21 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) with their enormous
weapons and have the use of any two
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) or
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric)
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) of
each spell level per day. A titan lair will contain an additional
3,000-18,000 gp.

##### Toads, Giant

will swallow
[halflings](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#halflings_1) and smaller
folk whole on any attack roll that exceeds the number required to hit by
4 or more. They can hop 18" every other
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns),
[swim](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#swimming), breath underwater,
and are 50% likely to be venomous.

##### Treants

are 20-30ft tall tree-[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men).
They are guardians of the ancient forests they inhabit and have little
interest in the affairs of short-lived races such as
[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men). If roused they are
dangerous enemies and will deal 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). They are
invulnerable to [normal
