weapons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-weapons) and suffer
one-half [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) from
magical weaponry other than
[axes](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#axes) but are vulnerable to
fire. Thrice per day a treant can awaken any other tree within 6". An
awakened tree fights exactly as another treant without the ability to
awaken others.

##### Trolls

are thin, loathsome humanoids with rubbery green skin. They would be
tall if they were not always hunched over. They have
[ogre](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ogres)-like
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) but rarely
employ anything more than tooth and claw so cause only 1-6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). They regenerate 3
[lost hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) per
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns), beginning three
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) after injury,
enabling even severed limbs to reattach or re-grow. The only way to
permanently slay a troll is to burn its remains or immerse it in acid.

##### Unicorns

are fierce, noble, magical steeds. They are reclusive creatures who will
tolerate contact only with a maiden of pure heart. If she is a valorous
warrior a unicorn may consent to serve as her steed, using its horn as a
lance when it charges. A unicorn saves as a 12th level
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user), is
able to sense enemies within 24", and can [dimension
door](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dimension-door) up to 36" once
each day.

##### Vampires

are dreadful and intelligent blood-sucking undead. Fortunately, they
must sleep during the day in a coffin containing soil from their
homeland. They are impervious to [normal
weaponry](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-weapons) and
regenerate 3 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) per
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) if injured. If reduced
to 0 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice)
they are not slain but forced to assume [gaseous
form](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#gaseous-form) and flee. They
can [polymorph](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#polymorph) into
[gaseous form](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#gaseous-form) or a
[giant bat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#bats-giant) at will and
can call forth and command 10-80
[bats](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#bats-giant), 2-12 [giant
rats](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rats-giant), or 1-10
[wolves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wolves).

Any [man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) enduring
eye contact with a vampire is subject to a [charm
person](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#charm-person) spell with a
−2 adjustment to the [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws). Once a victim
is charmed the vampire can bite at the neck with impunity, draining two
experience levels per [turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns)
of gorging. Any
[heroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types)/[superheroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) so slain by a
vampire will arise the next night as a vampire enslaved to the
[monster](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2) who made him.
Others so slain arise instead as
[ghouls](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ghouls). Vampires are
destroyed only by direct sunlight, immersion in running water, or a
wooden stake through the heart. They can be held at bay by a strongly
presented Cross, the smell of fresh garlic, or the face of a mirror.

##### Weasels, Giant

are cunning hunters adept at moving through tunnels and crawl
[spaces](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#space-required) in fierce
packs. When an attack roll exceeds the number required to hit by 4 or
more a [giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants) weasel bites
and holds on, gorging on the victim’s blood and draining him of 1-4 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) the following
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) and each
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) thereafter, until it
has sapped 1 point for each of its own [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice).
Any victim reduced to nil
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) is slain.

##### Wight Apes

are so called for their pale coloration and dread demeanor. They occur
in small bands in dense jungles and around ruined catacombs. They are
larger and more aggressive than regular
[apes](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#apes) and have a taste for
[man](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men)-flesh. Worse yet, they
possess a malign cunning employing rocks and stones as tools and their
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) is such that
they cause 1-11 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) on a hit.

##### Wights

are accursed undead that drain one experience level on a hit. They
dislike [light](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#light_2) and their
attack rolls and
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
checks are penalized by −2 in daylight. They are impervious to [normal
weaponry](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-weapons) unless it
is silvered, but magic weapons will do them double
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). Any
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) slain by a
wight will arise on the following night as a wight.

##### Wolves

occur primarily in cold regions and hunt in packs.

##### Wolves, Giant

includes dire [wolves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wolves) and
wargs, both being larger than their
[normal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types) kin. Wargs
are especially cunning and evil and are 20% likely to speak the common
tongue and always speak the chaotic tongue. They can be ridden by
[goblins](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#goblins) although this
will reduce either to 12"
[movement](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) and
a single attack roll each
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) even versus
[normal-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types).

##### Woolly Mammoths

are enormous, hairy, elephant-like mammals that occur in herds in arctic
regions. They are more aggressive than
[mastodons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#mastodons) and are
invulnerable to cold. They cause 3-18 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) by charging,
trampling, crushing, or goring with their mighty tusks.

##### Woolly Rhinoceroses

are enormous, hairy, rhinoceros-like mammals that occur in arctic
regions. They have poor eyesight but excellent hearing and are inclined
to attack anything that approaches or spooks them. They are invulnerable
to cold and cause 4-14 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) by charging,
trampling, or crushing.

##### Wraiths

are dreadful undead that exist more in the spirit
[world](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#creating-a-world) and less
in the physical. They dislike
[light](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#light_2) and their attack
rolls and
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
checks are penalized by −2 in daylight.
[Normal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types)
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) must check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
immediately if attacked by a wraith, while evil sorts fighting alongside
one receive +1 on their
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
[dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-dice_1). They drain one
experience level on a hit. They are impervious to [normal
weaponry](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-weapons) unless it
is silvered, although silver weapons will do them only half
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). Any
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) slain by a
wraith will arise on the following night as a wraith.

##### Wyverns

are [dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons)-like
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2) with only one
pair of legs, no [breath
weapon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon), and a deadly
venomous stinger in the tail which is very agile and can strike all
around. An attack roll that exceeds the number required to hit by 4 or
more, or is a 20 in any case, indicates a stinger attack; otherwise, it
is a bite and claw attack that causes 3-8 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage).

##### Yellow Mold

is a deadly fungus found clinging to walls, floors, and ceilings
underground. It is impervious to most attacks and can only be
exterminated with fire. It dissolves wood in one
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) and causes 1-6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) per
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) to flesh but has no
effect on metal or stone. If it is disturbed there is a 50% chance a
toxic spore cloud will burst forth causing
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) within 1" to
save [versus poison](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#poison) or die.

##### Zombies

are mindless undead brought forth by a
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) or
[anti-cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-anti-cleric) to
serve some wicked purpose. These can carry
[shields](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields) or wear
[armor](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields), or both,
which would improve AC to 8 or 7, respectively. They are unaffected by
[normal missiles](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-missiles),
require no sustenance, and need never check
[morale](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks).

## Treasures

### Treasure Types

When a [monster](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2) lair is
discovered it will contain the
[monsters’](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2)
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) hoard (if any)
according to its stated
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) type. The
referee should [dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-dice_1)
for each category of
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) (copper,
silver, gold, etc.) separately, firstly checking to determine if the
category of [treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) is
present in the hoard and secondly, if it is present, to determine
quantity.

The percentage figures are the chance that the category will be present
and the range figures are quantites. For example,
[orcs](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#orcs) have [treasure
type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasure-types) C so there is
a 17% chance their lair will contain 1,000-12,000 cp, a 33% chance their
lair will contain 1,000-4,000 sp, a 33% chance their lair will contain
1-4 gems, a 33% chance their lair will contain 1 piece of jewelry, and a
17% chance their lair will contain 2 items from the “Any
[Treasures](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures)” table.

Note that [monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2) do
not carry [treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures)
outside their lair unless stated otherwise in the [explanation of
monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-monsters).

The value of gems and pieces of jewelry are individually determined.

Where maps or specific types of magic items are indicated the referee
should [dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-dice_1) on the
appropriate [treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures)
tables.

## Explanation of Treasures

Maps reveal the location of a
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) trove which
may contain valuables, or magic items, or both. A map will indicate the
type and approximate worth of the
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures), which can be
determined randomly or by the referee. A map will usually be cryptic or
obscured—requiring the use of a [comprehend
languages](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#comprehend-languages)
spell or the expertise of a canny
[thief](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-thief-optional-class)
(if these are used) to decipher. The
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) indicated
therein will be guarded by appropriate
[traps](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#tricks-and-traps) and/or
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2).

### Armor and Shields

A suit of magical armor or an enchanted shield will reduce an opponent’s
attack rolls by an amount equal to its adjustment. Thus, a suit of plate
armor +1 will cause enemies to attack at −1, a shield +2 will cause
enemies to attack at −2, and so on. If a character wearing magical armor
also carries an enchanted shield of greater potency, its greater
adjustment is applicable on any
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) he throws a 5 or 6 on
a six-sided die.

### Miscellaneous Magic Items

These items are usable by all characters unless noted otherwise.

##### Amulet of Proof Against Detection

An amulet that blocks all forms of magical detection including by
[crystal ball](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#crystal-ball),
[locate object](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#locate-object),
[detect
invisibility](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#detect-invisibility),
[sixth sense](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#sixth-sense), and
[witch eye](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#witch-eye). It is
ineffective against mundane detection, however.

##### Bag of Holding

An amazing sack that can hold up to 10,000 coins and appear only
partially full and weigh only 50 lb. Anything not wider than 3ft × 3ft
can be fit into it.

##### Boots of Elvenkind

Elvish footwear that enables the wearer to
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) almost
completely silently.

##### Boots of Levitation

Empowers the wearer to
[levitate](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#levitate) as per the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) spell
of the same name but with unlimited duration.

##### Boots of Speed

Anyone so shod may run at up to 24" for a full day after which he must
[rest](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#resting) for a day.

##### Boots of Striding and Springing

The wearer can sustain his full
[speed](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#speed) indefinitely without
need of [rest](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#resting).
Furthermore, thrice per day he can make a great leap up to 6" forward or
2" directly upward or backward, landing soundly on his feet.

##### Cloak of Displacement

The wearer of this cloak appears slightly displaced in time and
[space](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#space-required) adding +2 to
[saving throws](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws)
[versus wands and
rays](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wands-and-rays) and adjusting
physical attack rolls by −2.

##### Cloak of Elvenkind

A wondrous cloak that renders the wearer nearly invisible.

##### Crystal Ball

Employable by
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) only,
these provide vision of a desired place, person, or object. Great
[distance](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#encounter-distance_3) and
unfamiliarity will decrease the chance that the subject can be located,
however. Except as noted below, the other senses will remain
unsatisfied.
[Spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) such
as [read magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#read-magic),
[darkvision](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#darkvision), and
[detect
invisibility](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#detect-invisibility)
will affect what may be seen but no spell or spell-like effect can be
[cast](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory)
through a crystal ball. Most crystal balls enable only
[clairvoyance](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#clairvoyance) but 1
in 6 will also permit the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) to hear
thoughts exactly as does the [sixth
sense](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#sixth-sense) spell. These may
be used no more than thrice per day without risk of being
[feebleminded](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#feeblemind) and each
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) of usage requires a
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) of
[rest](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#resting) thereafter.

##### Drums of Panic

This pair of great drums are too large to be carried by a
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) but may be
transported on a wagon or beast of burden. When beaten these drums will
panic all living things at least 2" but not more than 12" away.
[Heroic-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types) are
allowed a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell) to resist;
[superheroic-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
are unaffected. Panicked creatures will flee at their fastest rate for a
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### Efreeti Bottle

The [efreet](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#an-efreeti) trapped in
this bottle will grudgingly serve whomever should free him (and no
other) for a year and a day.

##### Flying Broomstick

This magical broom is employable by
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) only
and can [fly](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fly) at 24" per
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) with one rider, or at
18" per [turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) with two
riders.

##### Flying Carpet

Can carry one or two riders at 24" per
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) or three riders at 12"
per [turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### Gauntlets of Ogre Power

The wearer of these gains
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) equal to an
[ogre](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ogres), enabling him to
perform feats of great
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) and to deal +2
[hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice)
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) in
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat).

##### Girdle of Giant’s Might

The wearer of this wide leather girdle gains
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) equal to a
[hill giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants-hill). He is
capable of mighty feats of
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) including
hurling rocks and dealing 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) in
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat).

##### Magical Helms

are not considered to be
[armor](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields). They do
not adjust [armor class](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#melee) and
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) are
not restricted from wearing them. Should these be worn in battle the
referee may assume that 1 blow in 6 is aimed at the head. If that blow
should connect the helm is struck and requires a successful [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) to avoid being
smashed.

##### Helm of Alignment Change

If worn, this [helm](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magical-helms)
immediately causes lawful persons to become chaotic and vice versa.
Neutral persons are 50% likely to change either way. Removing the
[helm](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magical-helms) thereafter
will not revert the subject’s
[alignment](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#alignment)—this can only
be accomplished by [a wish](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wishes).
Of course the affected person will resist such efforts to the utmost of
his
[ability](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-abilities).

##### Helm of Comprehend Languages and

Magic The wearer can read any magical inscriptions,
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) maps, and
mundane writing.

##### Helm of Telepathy

This [helm](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magical-helms) enables
the wearer to probe subjects within 9" in exactly the same manner as the
[sixth sense](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#sixth-sense) spell.
Additionally, the wearer can implant a mental suggestion in any
intelligent subject so sensed. If a suggestion is attempted the referee
throws a
[reaction](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
check for the subject, adjusting the result by +2. A positive or better
[reaction](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
indicates that the subject will enact any reasonable (according to his
[alignment](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#alignment)) suggestion.

##### Helm of Teleportation

This [helm](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magical-helms) grants
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) only
the ability to
[teleport](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#teleportation) up to
three times per day as per the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) spell.
If the [magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
also has the
[teleport](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#teleportation) spell
memorized that spell will not be erased from memory when
[cast](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-casting-from-memory)
for so long as this
[helm](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magical-helms) is worn.

##### Horn of Blasting

A blast upon this great horn delivers 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) to all living
things within a cone-shaped area of effect 10" long and up to 3" wide.
Survivors are deafened for a
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) and any
[buildings](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#building) or
fortifications suffer structural
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage).

##### Medallion of Thoughts

Grants the wearer use of the [sixth
sense](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#sixth-sense) spell except
that there is 1 chance in 6 it will fail to perceive any particular
subject.

##### Mirror of Life Trapping

A [shield](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#armor-and-shields)-sized
mirror that
[traps](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#tricks-and-traps) any
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) or undead who
sees his own reflection at 1" or closer. It is 90% likely that an unwary
subject will see his reflection in good
[light](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#light_2), but only 10%
likely if he is wary of the mirror’s power. A
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can
gaze into a mirror safely with a secret command word or the use of a
[gazeback](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#gazeback) spell. The
mirror can contain 15-20 prisoners at one time with each being held
individually in a private null dimension. Those so imprisoned remain
unharmed but are completely powerless therein. A
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) can
call any prisoner to the surface of the mirror to converse, and if
desired, can free them from the mirror. Breaking the mirror will free
all prisoners simultaneously.

##### Object of Commanding Elementals

These four objects are usable by
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) only,
each conjuring an
[elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals) of a
particular type. The conjuration requires a full
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) of preparation and
another of invocation. The
[elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals) brought
forth will then have 12 [hit
dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) and
be subject to the
[magic-user’s](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) will
exactly as per the [invoke
elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#invoke-elemental) spell.

-   Stone of Controlling Earth Elementals
-   Brazier of Commanding Fire Elementals
-   Censer of Controlling Air Elementals
-   Bowl of Commanding Water Elementals

##### Scarab of Protection

Affords the wearer absolute immunity from disintegration, finger of
death, level drain, [vorpal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#vorpal)
swords, and [curses](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses). The
scarab will nullify 2-12 such attacks before crumbling to dust.

### Miscellaneous Weaponry

##### Arrows and Bolts

(50% chance of either) are usable by
[fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) only. The
magical adjustment applies both to attack and
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) rolls. The attack
adjustment is cumulative with that of any magical
[bow](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#bows) so a +1 arrow fired from
a +1 longbow would have a total attack adjustment of +2.

##### Axes

(50% chance of either battle axe or hand axe) are usable by
[fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) only. The
magical adjustment for battle axes applies to both attack and
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) rolls, but that for
hand axes applies to attack rolls only. Hand axes can be hurled up to 3"
as a medium range
[missile](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#missile-fire) attack.

##### Bows

are equally likely to be crossbows, longbows, or short bows; all are
usable by [fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter)
only. The magical adjustment of these applies to attack rolls only.

##### Daggers

are usable by
[fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter),
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user), and
[thieves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-thief-optional-class)
(if these are used). The magical adjustment applies to attack rolls
only. The second adjustment (if given) is applicable to attack rolls
versus a specific type. Daggers can be hurled up to 3" as a medium range
[missile](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#missile-fire) attack.

##### Flails and Maces

are usable by
[fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) and
[clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric). The magical
adjustment applies to
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) rolls only.

##### Morning Stars are

usable by [fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter)
only. The magical adjustment applies to
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) rolls only.

##### Short Swords

are usable by
[fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) and
[thieves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-thief-optional-class)
(if these are used). The magical adjustment applies to attack rolls
only. The second adjustment (if given) is applicable to attack rolls
versus a specific type.

##### Spears

are usable by
[fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) only. The
magical adjustment applies to attack rolls only but they can be hurled
up to 3" as a medium range
[missile](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#missile-fire) attack, and
three [men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men) can fight in a
defensive spear wall across a 10ft wide passage. Spears can also be set
against a charging foe to cause 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) on impact.

##### War Hammers

are usable by
[fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) and
[clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) and the
magical adjustment applies to
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) rolls only. These
can be hurled up to 3" as a medium range
[missile](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#missile-fire) attack.

##### War Hammer +3

In the hands of a
[fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) or
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) this weapon
adds +3 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) to
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). In the hands of a
[dwarf](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dwarfs_1), however, it
causes 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) against all foes
except [giants](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants), against
which it causes 5-15 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage). Additionally, a
[dwarf](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dwarfs_1) can throw the [war
hammer](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#war-hammers) +3 up to 6" and
it will automatically [fly](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fly)
back to his hand.

### Potions

A potion flask contains exactly enough fluid to cause the prescribed
effect, although a small sip may be tasted without altering its
efficacy. The duration of any temporary effect is 7-12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) unless stated
otherwise.

##### Abbreviation

Quaffing the full [potion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#potions)
will reduce a person to one-twelfth size. Thus, a 6ft tall
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) would shrink
to 6in. Consuming a lesser part will have a proportionally lesser
effect.

##### Animal Mastery

The imbiber gains control over 3-18 small animals, 2-12 medium sized
animals, or 1-6 large animals. Only
[normal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types) animal-types
can be controlled.

##### Curing

Restores 2-7 [lost hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice).

##### Deception

Causes the imbiber to believe the effect is whatever he desired it to be
or a randomly determined
[potion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#potions) effect determined
by the referee.

##### Dragon Mastery

The imbiber gains control over up to three
[dragons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) who fail to save
[versus spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell). Each
[potion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#potions) affects one type
of [dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons) as determined
by the referee.

##### Exaggeration

Quaffing the full [potion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#potions)
will enlarge a person to four times size. Thus, a 6ft tall
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) would grow to
24ft. Consuming a lesser part will have a proportionally lesser effect.

##### Extra Curing

Quaffing the full [potion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#potions)
restores 6-21 [lost hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice).
Taking a one-third part of it will restore 1-6 [lost hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice).

##### Flight

Consumption of this
[potion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#potions) has the same
effect as a [fly](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fly) spell except
that it lasts for 7-12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### Gaseous Form

The imbiber becomes a cohesive, mobile cloud of gas that can penetrate
any non-airtight
[space](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#space-required). However,
anything worn or carried drops to a heap on the floor.

##### Giant Mastery

The imbiber gains control over up to four
[giants](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants) who fail to save
[versus spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell). Each
[potion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#potions) affects only one
type of [giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants), as
determined by the referee.

##### Giant’s Strength

Grants [strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) equal to
a [hill giant](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants-hill)
including hurling rocks and causing 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) per hit.

##### Haste

Imbues the imbiber with the same effect as the
[haste](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#haste) spell except that it
lasts for 2-7 [turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### Heroism

Causes an ordinary
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) to function as
a [heroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types)
[fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) in all
respects. Leveled
[fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) are also
temporarily increased as follows:

##### Inviolability

Grants invulnerability to [normal
weaponry](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-weapons) and
improves [saving
throws](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) by +2 for
7-12 [turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### Invisibility

Drinking this [potion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#potions)
produces the same effect as the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
[invisibility](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#invisibility) spell
for 7-12 [turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### Mastery Over Men

The imbiber gains control over 2-12
[normal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types)
[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men), 1-6
[heroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types)
[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men), or 1
[superheroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
[man](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men) as per the [charm
person](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#charm-person) spell. [Saving
throws](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) are
applicable.

##### Plant Mastery

The imbiber gains control over ordinary plants within a 6" diameter or
1-6 ooze-types (including slimes, oozes, and puddings).

##### Poison

Even a sip is fatal unless a [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
poison](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#poison) is successful.

##### Polymorph

Produces the same effect as the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
[polymorph](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#polymorph) spell except
that it lasts only 7-12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### Resistance to Fire

Grants invulnerability to ordinary fire and adjusts [saving
throws](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) versus
magical fire, including
[fireball](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fireball) and [red
dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons-red) breath, by +2.
Any fire [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) sustained
is reduced by 1 [hit
point](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) per
die regardless.

##### Sixth Sense

Drinking this [potion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#potions)
produces the same effect as the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) [sixth
sense](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#sixth-sense) spell for 7-12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### Treasure Detection

Quaffing this [potion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#potions)
enables the detection of any
[treasure](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treasures) worth 5,000 gp
or more within 36". It is not blocked by lead, stone, or anything else.

##### Undead Mastery

The imbiber gains control over 2-12
[normal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types) undead or 1-6
[heroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types) undead as per
the [charm monster](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#charm-monster)
spell. The latter are allowed [saving
throws](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell).

##### Water Breathing

The imbiber can breathe comfortably underwater for 7-12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### Weightlessness

Imbibing this [potion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#potions) has
the same effect as the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
[levitate](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#levitate) spell for 7-12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### X-Ray Vision

Enables the imbiber to see through up to 10ft of stone or 6in of iron to
a [distance](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#encounter-distance_3)
of 6" for 7-12 [turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).
Everything will be revealed including
[traps](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#tricks-and-traps) and secret
places. The magic is obstructed by lead or gold and only a 1" × 1"
section of wall can be examined each
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

##### Youthfulness

Reduces the imbiber’s age by 10 years.

### Rings

Magic rings are usable by all characters though they must be worn in
order to function. One ring may be worn on each hand and these will have
a continual effect unless noted otherwise in the description.

##### Animal Mastery

The wearer may exert control over 3-18 small animals, 2-12 medium-sized
animals, or 1-6 large animals within 6" at any one time. Only ordinary
animal-types can be controlled.

##### Darkvision

The wearer can see in darkness as per the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
[darkvision](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#darkvision) spell for
so long as he wears this
[ring](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings).

##### Deception

Causes the wearer to believe the effect is whatever he originally
desired it to be or an effect determined by the referee.

##### Invisibility

The wearer becomes invisible as per the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
[invisibility](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#invisibility) spell
for so long as he wears this
[ring](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings).

##### Mastery Over Men

The wearer may exert control over 2-12
[normal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types)
[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men), 1-6
[heroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types)
[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men), or 1
[superheroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
[man](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men) within 6" at any time.
All are allowed [saving
throws](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell) in the same manner as
per the [charm person](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#charm-person)
spell.

##### Protection

The wearer’s [saving
throws](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) are adjusted
by +2 and any attack rolls that are targeted at him are adjusted by −2
for so long as he wears this
[ring](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings).

##### Regeneration

Causes the wearer to regain 1 [lost hit
point](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) each
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns). Severed limbs will
reattach or re-grow. If the wearer is reduced to 0 (or fewer) [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) he
will even return from the dead if he makes a successful [shock
survival](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#shock-survival) check.
Only fire or acid will destroy the wearer with certainty.

##### Resistance to Fire

Grants the wearer invulnerability to ordinary fire and adjusts [saving
throws](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) versus
magical fire, including
[fireball](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fireball) and [red
dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons-red) breath, by +2.
Any fire [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) sustained
is reduced by 1 [hit
point](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) per
die regardless.

##### Spell Storing

A [ring](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings) of this type can
store 1-6
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) of
either the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user),
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric), or
[anti-cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-anti-cleric) sort
with a throw of 1-4, 5, or 6 on a six-sided die, respectively. The
anti-clerical [rings](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings) are
harmful to [clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) and
vice versa. Whether there are stored
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) in
the [ring](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings), and what
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) they
are, should be determined randomly if such a
[ring](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings) is found. Anyone
(including a non-spell caster) who places this
[ring](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings) on his finger
immediately knows which
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells), if
any, are stored therein and may invoke them. Each stored spell can be
invoked once before it is expended. The
[ring](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings) can only be recharged
by a [magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user),
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric), or
[anti-cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-anti-cleric),
respectively.

##### Spell Turning

Any spell targeted specifically at the wearer of this
[ring](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings) is 80% likely to be
turned back at the caster. For each experience level the spell caster
has beyond the 4th it is 10% less likely that his spell will be turned.

##### Telekinesis

The wearer is able to shift loads up to 200 lb at a rate of 12" to
anywhere within a 12" radius simply by concentrating.

##### The Djinn

The wearer may call forth a
[djinni](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#a-djinni) who is
permanently bound to serve whoever wears the
[ring](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings). The
[djinni](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#a-djinni) is as are all
[monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2) of its type.

##### Water Walking

Enables the wearer to walk on water as if he were walking on dry land.

##### Weariness

The wearer is reduced to half his usual
[strength](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#strength) and is affected
by a [slow](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#slow) spell for so long
as he wears this [ring](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings). It
can only be removed by a [remove
curse](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#remove-curse) spell or [a
wish](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wishes).

##### Wishes

Grants either 3 or 1-6 (50% chance of either) wishes to the wearer. A
wish is powerful magic indeed but only the most literal interpretation
of a wish will be honored.

A wish must be uttered in one breath. It can be used to
[heal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#healing) a player, to restore
him to life, to lift
[curses](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses), to [dispel
magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-magic), and so on.
[Ability](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-abilities)
scores can be restored to normal or raised by 1 point (up to 18). A
[lost](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#becoming-lost) experience
level can be restored but a new experience level cannot be added. Any
wealth or object brought to hand will come from the nearest source and
the rightful owner will not be pleased with this theft.

The referee should adjudicate the effects of a wish carefully. A wish
that all [orcs](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#orcs) should die,
for example, might have no effect given that
[orcs](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#orcs) are mortal and will die
eventually in any case.

##### X-Ray Vision

Enables the wearer to see through up to 10ft of stone or 6in of iron to
a [distance](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#encounter-distance_3)
of 6". Everything will be revealed including
[traps](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#tricks-and-traps) and secret
places. The magic is obstructed by lead or gold and only a 1" × 1"
section of wall can be examined each
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).

### Spellbooks and Scrolls

Scrolls are either [spell
scrolls](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-scrolls),
[wards](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wards), or
[curses](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses). Each type can be
identified by anyone who can read. [Spell
scrolls](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-scrolls) are usable
only by the appropriate magical types and
[curses](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#curses) are triggered as
soon as they are identified.

#### Spell Scrolls

Spell
[scrolls](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spellbooks-and-scrolls)
are of the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user),
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric), or
[anti-cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-anti-cleric) sort
when a 1-4, 5, or 6 is thrown on a six-sided die, respectively. A spell
[scroll](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spellbooks-and-scrolls)
will contain 1-3
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) with
the level and name of each spell being determined randomly. A spell
invoked from a
[scroll](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spellbooks-and-scrolls) is
as per the minimum caster level necessary to memorize the spell.

#### Wards

Wards function as does the [circle of protection from
evil](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#circle-of-protection-from-evil)
spell except that they are effective against a specific type and number
of [monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2) and have a
duration of one hour.

##### Ward against Elementals

Effective against a single
[elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals) of any type.

##### Ward against Lycanthropes

Effective against 2-12
[lycanthropes](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#lycanthropes) of any
type.

##### Ward against Magic

Effective against all magic in a 1" sphere about the invoker for one
hour in the same manner as the [anti-magic
shield](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#anti-magic-shield) spell.

##### Ward against Undead

Effective against 4-24
[normal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#normal-types) undead, 2-12
[heroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#heroic-types) undead, or
1-6 [superheroic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#superheroic-types)
undead.

#### Curses

Curses will affect the invoker and any
[man-types](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) within 15ft.

### Staves & Wands

Staves are employable by
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) and
[clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) as weapons or
for firing spell-like effects as an 8th level caster. A staff holds up
to 200 charges but will have only 10-200 charges when found.

Wands are employable by
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) only
and will fire spell-like effects as a 6th level caster. A wand holds up
to 100 charges but will have only 10-100 charges when found.

Each use of a spell-like effect drains one charge unless stated
otherwise.

##### Serpent Staff

Usable by [clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric)
only, this [staff](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands)
adds +1 to attack and
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) rolls. On a
successful attack the
[cleric](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric) can expend one
charge to transmute the
[staff](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) into a
mass of writhing serpents that coil about the target preventing a
[man](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men)-sized opponent from
attacking for 1-4 [turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns).
After this period the serpents slither back to their owner and return to
[staff](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) form.

##### Staff of Healing

Usable by [clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric)
only, this [staff](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands)
cures 2-7 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) at
a touch. It will function only once on any one person each day.

##### Staff of Mastery

This [staff](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) has
the combined powers of [plant
mastery](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#plant-mastery), [animal
mastery](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#animal-mastery), and
[mastery over
men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#mastery-over-men).

##### Staff of Power

Employable by
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) only,
this [staff](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) can
invoke a [lightning
bolt](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#lightning-bolt),
[fireball](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fireball), or cone of
intense cold 6" long and up to 2" wide. Each of these cause 8-48 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) but a successful
[saving throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) will
reduce this [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) by
half. Additionally, the
[staff](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) may cause
[continuous
light](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#continuous-light), [wall of
fire](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wall-of-fire), and
[telekinesis](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#telekinesis) (up to
250 lb). If used in [combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat)
it performs as a [staff of
smiting](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staff-of-smiting).

As a last resort the wielder may perform a final strike, thereby
breaking the
[staff](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) and
releasing all its remaining energy. The resulting blast causes 1 point
of [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) per remaining
charge to all creatures within 3".

##### Staff of Smiting

Uses no charges but causes 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) on a hit.

##### Staff of Sorcery

Employable by
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) only,
this [staff](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) has
all the functions of the [staff of
power](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staff-of-power) and can
additionally invoke a whirlwind (as a
[djinn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#a-djinni)),
[invisibility](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#invisibility),
[invoke elemental](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#invoke-elemental)
(8 HD), paralysis (as the
[wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands)),
[passwall](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#passwall), [wall of
ice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wall-of-ice), and
[web](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#web).

##### Staff of Wasting

A successful hit causes 1-6 points of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) and ages the target
by one decade. This has little impact upon
[elves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elves_1) but is a terrible
toll upon [men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men).

##### Wand of Cancellation

This [wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) will
[dispel magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-magic) exactly
as per the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) [dispel
magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dispel-magic) spell.

##### Wand of Detecting Enemies

Use of this [wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands)
will reveal anyone within 6" who is hostile or malicious toward the
wielder.

##### Wand of Detecting Magic

Use of this [wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands)
will reveal the presence of any ongoing magic
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells) or
enchanted objects within 2". Expending a second charge will reveal the
general nature of one specific spell or enchanted item.

##### Wand of Detecting Metal

Use of this [wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands)
will reveal the location and type of any metal of at least 100 lb (2,000
coins) mass within 2".

##### Wand of Detecting Secrets

Use of this [wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands)
will reveal any secret or concealed
[doors](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#doors) or passages within
2".

##### Wand of Detecting Traps

Use of this [wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands)
will reveal any and all
[traps](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#tricks-and-traps) within 2".

##### Wand of Fear

This [wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) will
produce a cone of panic exactly as per the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
[fear](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fear) spell.

##### Wand of Fireball

This [wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) will
invoke a 6 [dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-dice_1)
[fireball](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fireball) exactly as per
the [magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
[fireball](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#fireball) spell.

##### Wand of Ice

This [wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) will
produce a cone of intense cold 6" long and up to 2" wide which causes 6
[dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-dice_1) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) to everyone in the
area. A [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus breath
weapons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#breath-weapon) will reduce
this [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) by half.

##### Wand of Lightning Bolt

This [wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) will
invoke a 6 [dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-dice_1)
[lightning bolt](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#lightning-bolt)
exactly as per the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
[lightning bolt](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#lightning-bolt)
spell.

##### Wand of Paralysis

This [wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) will
invoke a 9" long, baleful ray which will paralyze any single
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) for 2-12
[turns](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) unless he makes a
successful [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
wands](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wands-and-rays).

##### Wand of Phantasm

This [wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands) will
generate an [illusion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#illusions)
exactly as per the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
[phantasm](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#phantasm) spell, except
that the wielder can
[move](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#time-and-movement_2) at a
normal walk while maintaining the
[illusion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#illusions). Breaking the
wielder’s concentration will end the
[illusion](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#illusions).

##### Wand of Polymorph

Use of this [wand](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#staves-and-wands)
enables the wielder to
[polymorph](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#polymorph) himself or
others exactly as per the
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
[polymorph](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#polymorph) and [baleful
polymorph](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#baleful-polymorph)
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells).

### Magic Swords

Magic swords are usable by
[fighters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) only. In
addition to their attack and
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) adjustments the
greatest magic swords also have
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence_1),
[alignment](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#alignment),
[purpose](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#purpose), and the
possibility of spell-like
[powers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#powers). The second magical
adjustment (if given) is applicable to attack and
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) rolls against the
specified target types. The first magical adjustment applies to attack
and [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) rolls against
all other targets.

##### Cursed

Subtracts from attack rolls and will always (magically) appear in hand.
The player will have great difficulty ridding himself of this weapon.

##### Versus Man-types

Causes additional [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage)
to one specific
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) including
[men](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#men),
[elves](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elves_1),
[dwarfs](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dwarfs_1), and
[halflings](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#halflings_1).

##### Versus Lycanthropes

Causes additional [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage)
to [lycanthropes](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#lycanthropes) and
shape-shifters.

##### Versus Enchanted

Causes additional [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage)
to [magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) and
magic-using [monsters](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#monsters_2).

##### Versus Giants

Causes additional [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage)
to [giants](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#giants).

##### Versus Dragons

Causes additional harm to one specific type of
[dragon](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons). If this sword is
chaotic it is especially harmful to [golden
dragons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons-golden). If this
sword is lawful it is especially harmful to either white, black, green,
blue, or [red dragons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons-red);
otherwise, it will be harmful to any one type.

##### Versus Regenerating

Causes additional [damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage)
to any regenerating creatures including
[trolls](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#trolls),
[clerics](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-cleric), and
characters with regenerating
[rings](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings) or swords.

##### Flametongue

This sword is continually afire with magical flames. It deals +3
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) to creatures of
cold and those vulnerable to fire including
[mummies](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#mummies),
[treants](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#treants), and [white
dragons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons-white).

##### Frostbrand

This sword glimmers with frigid blue
[light](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#light_2). It deals +3
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) to creatures of
fire and those vulnerable to cold including [fire
elementals](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#elementals-fire),
[efreet](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#an-efreeti), and [red
dragons](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#dragons-red).

##### Holy

This sword is always lawful regardless of its
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence_1). In
the hands of a lawful
[fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) it is a sword
+2, +4 versus chaotics and functions as a [ring of spell
turning](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-turning) against
chaotic spell casters; otherwise, it functions only as a sword +2.

##### Unholy

this sword is always chaotic regardless of its
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence_1). In
the hands of a chaotic
[fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) it is a sword
+2, +4 versus lawfuls and functions as a [ring of spell
turning](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell-turning) against
lawful spell casters; otherwise, it functions only as a sword +2.

##### Vorpal

This sword is always neutral, regardless of its
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence_1). In
the hands of a neutral
[fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) any attack
roll that exceeds the number required to hit by 4 or more, or is a 20 in
any case, will decapitate a
[man-type](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#man-types) who fails to
save [versus wands](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wands-and-rays);
otherwise, it functions only as a sword +2.

When a [magic sword](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magic-swords)
is indicated the referee should
[dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-dice_1) on the [magic
swords](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magic-swords) table and then
throw two six-sided
[dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-dice_1) to determine
whether the sword is intelligent. A result of 2-6 indicates a
non-intelligent sword much like other magical weaponry. A result of 7 or
more indicates an intelligent sword with the possibility of additional
[powers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#powers).

#### Intelligence

Some [magic swords](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magic-swords)
are intelligent as determined by a throw of two six-sided
[dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-dice_1).

Dicing 6 or less indicates a regular magic weapon. Dicing 7 or more
indicates an intelligent, living thing with its own motivations and
personality. The referee should play it as he would any other non-player
character, bearing in mind the sword may not be friendly to its
wielder—this being determined by an initial
[reaction](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#reaction-and-morale-checks)
check and the developing relationship between them.

#### Communication

An intelligent sword is able to communicate. Empathic communication is
via physical hints such as pointing, leaning, shaking, and vibrating.
Verbal communication is via an audible voice spoken in any
[language](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#many-languages) the sword
knows. An intelligent sword capable of verbal communication will always
know its [alignment](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#alignment)
tongue and a number of additional
[languages](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#many-languages)
determined by two six-sided
[dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-dice_1).

The most intelligent [magic
swords](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magic-swords) are able to
[read magic](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#read-magic) and to
communicate telepathically in addition to their ability to speak.

#### Alignment

All intelligent [magic
swords](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magic-swords) are either
lawful, neutral, or chaotic. A
[holy](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#holy) sword is always lawful,
an [unholy](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#unholy) sword is always
chaotic, and a [vorpal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#vorpal)
sword is always neutral, regardless of its
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence_1).

##### Alignment Damage

Any character who willingly handles an enchanted sword of a different
[alignment](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#alignment) will suffer
1-6 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) for each step its
[alignment](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#alignment) is removed
from his. For example, a lawful player will suffer 2-12 [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice) of
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage) if he handles a
chaotic sword. A character contacting a magical sword unwillingly or
under instruction is spared half this
[damage](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#damage).

#### Ego

All intelligent swords have an ego. The higher a sword’s ego the more
challenging it will be to master. A sword’s ego rating is determined by
throwing two six-sided
[dice](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-dice_1) and adjusting the
result by +1 for each additional
[language](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#many-languages) or
[power](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#powers) the sword possesses
(whichever is greater).

#### Powers

Intelligent swords will possess a number of additional powers and
exceptional powers. The referee should roll on the [Magic
Sword](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magic-swords) Powers table
and, if necessary, the [Magic
Sword](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magic-swords) Exceptional
Powers table to determine each of these functions.

The wielder is required to hold the sword unsheathed and to concentrate
for a [turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) in order to
invoke any of these powers. Only a single power may be used each
[turn](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#turns) but they can otherwise
be used thrice per day, with the exception of regeneration (which is
continuous) and [wishes](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wishes)
(which can be used a total of 3 or 1-6 times).

Unless noted otherwise, these powers are as the equivalent
[magic-user](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user)
[spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#explanation-of-spells).

A sword with the life stealing power can invoke a finger of death once
per day and is always chaotic. If it is a
[holy](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#holy) or
[vorpal](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#vorpal) sword it is
declared an [unholy](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#unholy) sword
instead.

#### Purpose

The most potent [magic
swords](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magic-swords) have been
forged for a specific purpose.Should a sword have both 9 or more
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence_1) and 9
or more [ego](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ego) it is a purposed
sword. It will have the maximum
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence_1) and
[ego](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ego)—promote both to 12 but do
not add [powers](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#powers) if
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence_1) is
raised.

The purpose of such a sword is determined by dicing on the [Magic
Sword](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#magic-swords) Purpose table.

In all cases the purpose of a sword is according to its
[alignment](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#alignment). Thus, a
lawful sword purposed to destroy
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) is
purposed to destroy chaotic
[magic-users](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-magic-user) only.
A neutral purposed sword affects lawful and chaotic types equally.

-   A lawful sword will paralyze a purposed foe on a successful hit if
    he fails to save [versus
    petrification](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#paralysis-and-petrification).
-   A neutral sword will
    [feeblemind](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#feeblemind) a
    purposed foe on a successful hit if he fails to save [versus
    spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell). Use confused
    behaviour if already in
    [combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat).
-   A chaotic sword will slay a purposed foe on a successful hit if he
    fails to save [versus
    poison](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#poison).

#### Dominance

An intelligent sword also has a dominance rating which is the sum of its
[intelligence](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#intelligence_1) and
[ego](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#ego).

A sword may mentally wrestle for dominance over its wielder in order to
get its own way when any of the following (or similar) circumstances
arise:

-   Any character willingly draws or even touches the sword,
-   The sword’s [purposed](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#purpose)
    enemy appears,
-   Another magical sword is found,
-   The wielder is reduced to fewer than half of his [hit
    points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice).

Compare the sword’s dominance to the sum of the player character’s
[wisdom](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#wisdom),
[charisma](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#charisma), and
[fighter](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-fighter) level. The
player character adds 1-6 if he is fresh and uninjured but subtracts 1-6
if he has fewer than half of his total possible [hit
points](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-numbers-of-hit-dice).
The sword adds 2-12 if its
[alignment](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#alignment) differs from
the player character’s.

If there is any difference in the sword’s favor it gains control over
the character unless he makes a successful [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) [versus
spells](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#spell). If the difference is
6 or more no [saving
throw](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#saving-throws) is allowed.

Whenever a sword dominates its wielder it causes him to act in
accordance with its own goals. This means disposing of competing
weapons, entering into glorious (or ignoble)
[combat](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#combat), decorating itself
with bejeweled hilt-work or scabbards, surrendering itself to a superior
wielder who can better achieve its goals (or an inferior one whom it can
more easily dominate), or any other actions that serve its own end.
Domination is usually exerted for the duration of one such action.

## Afterword

Much has been written down and accounted for, but all the words in this
book are merely a foundation for what will ultimately be a fantasy game
[campaign](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#the-campaign) of the
referee’s own devising. He is encouraged to create liberally and
enthusiastically and to welcome input from his players. Their choices
and actions should [ring](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#rings)
true in the game
[world](http://ddo.immersiveink.com/dd.html#creating-a-world) so that it
thrives and invites further participation. With a living game in motion
the referee can derive considerable enjoyment from extending or altering
the rules to meet his own particular needs. In this case the referee is
cautioned to do so judiciously and with consistency.

Above all, referees and players alike are reminded that this is a game
and that games are meant to be fun.

Fight On!
